# Debug Journal - LOGH VII client handshake
Started: 2026-06-09T10:35:00Z
Goal: Capture a real LOGH VII Windows client handshake and advance the local server only from observed bytes.

## Environment snapshot (Phase 0)
- Runtime: Windows PE native binaries launched from `.omo/work/logh7-installed`.
- Entry: `G7Start.exe` with local `update.ini`; `G7MTClient.exe` spawned/connected to `127.0.0.1:47900`.
- Ports / sockets: HTTP update/resource server `127.0.0.1:4787`; gameplay TCP capture `127.0.0.1:47900`.
- Git HEAD: `a7b58784b0f1762e5e56d744930809b552ea1582`; working tree dirty.
- References read: `debugging/SKILL.md`, `references/runtimes/native-binary.md`, `references/methodology/00-setup.md`, `references/methodology/02-investigate.md`.

## Hypotheses
1. [OPEN] Server-first handshake - the client connects then waits for a login/lobby protocol greeting before sending `LobbyLoginRequest`; distinguishing evidence: a candidate server greeting makes the same client emit a non-empty payload in trace; if true, fix is: greeting schema.
2. [OPEN] Launcher session handoff - the local update path starts the client but does not provide the session/login state needed to send credentials; distinguishing evidence: updater-created files or process arguments differ between `G7Start.exe` and direct `G7MTClient.exe`; if true, fix is: launch config.
3. [OPEN] Frame format mismatch - the client closes because the server is silent or sends an invalid first frame length/type; distinguishing evidence: one malformed/empty probe closes without payload while a length-framed probe changes timing or payload; if true, fix is: frame parser.

## Failed hypothesis round counter
- Round 1: in progress.

## Findings

### 2026-06-09T11:35:00Z - G005 phase3 response probe artifacts
- Source: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-code0035-length-sweep.qa.txt`.
- Value: `0x0035` body len `0` -> `exchange_key_phase3: param2 length is illegal(checksum)`; len `1-7,12,20` -> `illegal param2`; len `8,16,24,32,48,64` -> `param2 length is illegal(encipher)`.
- Interpretation: `0x0035` is parsed through key-exchange phase3, and phase3 param2 has checksum plus block-aligned encipher length constraints.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms G005 H1 that short `LobbyLoginOK`-style responses are not enough; supports cipher-envelope investigation.

### 2026-06-09T11:45:00Z - G005 structured phase3 probe and transport schema
- Source: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-code0035-structured-probes.qa.txt` and jump-table entry `0x4b864c + (messageCode - 1) * 4`.
- Value: transport `0x0034` maps to internal `0x0405`; transport `0x0035` maps to internal `0x0406`; structured 8/16-byte `0x0035` bodies kept producing `exchange_key_phase3: param2 length is illegal(encipher)`, 12-byte bodies kept producing `illegal param2`.
- Interpretation: `0x0034/0x0035` are cipher transport codes distinct from lobby semantic codes `0x2000..0x2002`; first-field length guesses do not satisfy phase3.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms the server schema must expose cipher transport separately and must not emit a `0x2001` login success yet.

### 2026-06-09T11:55:00Z - G005 dispatch queue mapping
- Source: client jump table at `0x4b864c`, dispatch tail `0x4b852b..0x4b862e`.
- Value: `0x0034` jump-table target queues internal `0x0405`; `0x0035` jump-table target queues internal `0x0406`; both require flag `[edi + 0x35837e]` before queuing.
- Interpretation: `0x0034/0x0035` are transport messages gated by cipher-enabled state and map to internal queued message IDs, not lobby semantic IDs.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms the protocol schema needs a transport dispatch mapping separate from `messageCodes.login`.

### 2026-06-09T12:05:00Z - G005 adjacent transport runtime probe
- Source: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-adjacent-transport-probes.qa.txt`.
- Value: `0x0034` body lengths `0,8,32` and `0x0036` body lengths `0,8,32` each captured one 28-byte login request, sent the candidate response, then `recv_eof`; stderr was empty for all six cases.
- Interpretation: the distinctive `mpsCipherManager exchange_key_phase3` stderr is specific to `0x0035` among these adjacent transport probes.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms `0x0035` is the useful phase3 diagnostic path; adjacent codes do not currently advance or expose a richer error.

### 2026-06-09T12:15:00Z - G005 request-derived phase3 probe
- Source: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-request-derived-phase3-probes.qa.txt`.
- Value: `0x0035` body equal to the live request body length 24 produced `exchange_key_phase3: broken data`; request body plus eight zero bytes length 32 and request body repeated length 48 also produced `broken data`; sum-appended variants length 28 produced `illegal param2`; transformed/sliced variants produced `param2 length is illegal(encipher)`.
- Interpretation: phase3 accepts some request-body-shaped inputs far enough to reach a deeper broken-data check, but the server response still needs a nontrivial transform/checksum rather than echo.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms request-derived phase3 responses are closer than zero/static candidates but still do not advance the client.

### 2026-06-09T12:35:00Z - G005 static phase3 decoded payload layout
- Source: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-cipher-phase-disasm.txt`, phase3 function starting at `0x645660`.
- Value: phase3 decoded payload is parsed as network-order checksum, network-order encipher key length, encipher key data, network-order decipher key length, decipher key data, then a network-order sequence dword. The checksum comparison at `0x645905` covers `decodedPayload[2:]`, XORs little-endian dwords plus trailing bytes, then compares the network-order stored checksum with `high16 xor low16`.
- Interpretation: a valid `0x0035` response must pass the cipher vtable decode path first; only then can this decoded payload layout satisfy key material and checksum checks.
- Refutes/Confirms: refines G005 from broad response probing to a concrete key-exchange frame generation problem.

### 2026-06-09T12:55:00Z - G005 decoded payload raw-wire probe
- Source: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-decoded-phase3-raw-wire-probes.qa.txt`.
- Value: checksum-correct decoded payload `decoded_empty_keys_seq1` sent as raw `0x0035` body produced `exchange_key_phase3: illegal param2`; `decoded_short_keys_seq1` produced `exchange_key_phase3: param2 length is illegal(encipher)`.
- Interpretation: the decoded phase3 payload builder is not sufficient as raw wire output; server response generation still needs the cipher wrapper used before `0x645660`.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms `phase3WireEncoding` remains unresolved and prevents implementing a deterministic login-success response yet.

### 2026-06-09T13:10:00Z - G005 phase3 processing pipeline catalog
- Source: `tools/logh7_cipher.py`, `tools/tests/test_logh7_cipher.py`, and `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-cipher-phase-disasm.txt`.
- Value: decoded phase3 checksum/payload helpers are covered with fixed hex vectors, while the protocol catalog now records the phase3 vtable calls: raw param2 decode at `0x64568e` via `manager+0x04` slot `0x10`, encipher-key compare at `0x645792` via `manager+0x08` slot `0x08`, decipher-key apply at `0x64593f` via `manager+0x0c` slot `0x04`, and phase3 reply encode at `0x645a53` via `manager+0x04` slot `0x0c`.
- Interpretation: the data schema now separates decoded phase3 payload construction from raw TCP wire encoding. The next executable server response depends on resolving the decode/encode vtable implementation rather than sending decoded payload bytes directly.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms C003 schema progress for G005, but leaves C001/C002 pending because the real client still has not advanced past login.

### 2026-06-09T13:35:00Z - G005 child codec vtable resolution
- Source: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-cipher-vtable-targets.txt`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-cipher-manager-callers.txt`, and `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-child-codec-vtable.txt`.
- Value: phase manager vtable `0x74572c` has slot `0x0c -> 0x645660` and slot `0x10 -> 0x645a80`; manager constructor `0x6450e0` receives child codec pointers from caller `0x6128ea`; child codec constructor `0x613fc0` installs vtable `0x681fc8`; child slot `0x0c -> 0x614100`; child slot `0x10 -> 0x614460`. The `0x614460` decode path rejects non-8-byte-aligned lengths before entering the block transform.
- Interpretation: raw phase3 wire encoding is implemented by the child codec, not directly by the phase manager. The next implementation target is reproducing child slot `0x614460`/`0x614100` block transform.
- Refutes/Confirms: refines G005 C003 schema evidence and keeps C001/C002 pending because no supported raw `0x0035` response has advanced the client.

### 2026-06-09T14:05:00Z - G005 child codec block transform shape
- Source: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-child-codec-block-transform.txt`.
- Value: child decode `0x614460` requires input length divisible by 8, copies raw input to output, then loops over 8-byte blocks. Child encode `0x614100` zero-pads non-aligned input to the next 8-byte boundary before the same block transform family. Key setup `0x613ad0` de-obfuscates a 18-dword P-array and 4 x 256-dword S-box tables by xor `0x91`; round helper `0x613f20` computes `((S1[b2] + S0[b3]) xor S2[b1]) + S3[b0]`; encode uses subkeys forward and decode uses subkeys reverse.
- Interpretation: the child codec is a Blowfish-like 16-round Feistel block cipher. Raw phase3 response generation now depends on wiring the right phase key material into this transform, not guessing frame lengths.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms G005 C003 schema progress; C001/C002 remain pending because no supported encrypted `0x0035` response has advanced the client.

### 2026-06-09T14:30:00Z - G005 child codec key flow
- Source: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-child-codec-key-flow.txt`.
- Value: child slot `0x04` wrapper `0x6140c0` calls key schedule `0x613ad0` with P-array pointer `codec+0x0c`, S-box pointer array `codec+0x10`, raw key bytes, and raw key length; on success it calls `0x614810`, which stores a copy of key bytes xor `0x17` at `codec+0x04` with length word at `codec+0x08`. `0x6148a0` reads the stored key and xor `0x17` restores it for comparison. Phase2 inbound applies decoded key bytes through `0x645478` to `manager+0x0c` slot `0x04`; phase3 compares through `0x645792` against `manager+0x08` slot `0x08` and applies decipher key at `0x64593f` to `manager+0x0c` slot `0x04`.
- Interpretation: the server needs to reproduce the raw key bytes expected by the child codec, not just the block transform shape. Stored key images are reversible xor `0x17`, but the live phase key bytes still need to be derived from phase2/phase3 payload flow.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms G005 C003 key-flow schema progress; C001/C002 remain pending because no supported encrypted `0x0035` response has advanced the client.

### 2026-06-09T14:55:00Z - G005 phase1 and phase2 decoded payload layouts
- Source: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-phase1-phase2-layouts.txt`.
- Value: phase1 manager slot `0x04` target `0x645180` builds decoded payload `checksum, keyLength, keyData, sequence`, computes checksum over payload after the first two bytes, then encodes through manager `+0x04` child codec slot `0x0c`. Phase2 manager slot `0x08` target `0x6452f0` decodes raw param through manager `+0x04` child codec slot `0x10`, then parses `checksum, remoteKeyLength, remoteKeyData, storedKeyLength, storedKeyData, sequence`; it applies remote key bytes through manager `+0x0c` slot `0x04` and emits a response containing remote key, local stored key, sequence, and checksum before encoding through manager `+0x04` slot `0x0c`.
- Interpretation: phase1/phase2/phase3 share the same decoded checksum family and length-prefixed key fields. The remaining work is executable server state: generating and encoding the correct phase sequence/key payloads.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms G005 C003 decoded-layout schema progress; C001/C002 remain pending because no supported encrypted response has advanced the client.

### 2026-06-09T13:10:00Z - G005 phase1 and phase2 decoded payload helpers
- Source: `tools/logh7_cipher.py`, `tools/tests/test_logh7_cipher.py`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-phase12-payload-red.txt`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-phase12-payload-green.txt`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-phase12-payload-protocol-endpoint-green.txt`.

### 2026-06-09T13:35:00Z - G005 child codec static tables
- Source: `tools/logh7_child_codec.py`, `tools/tests/test_logh7_cipher.py`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-child-static-tables-red.txt`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-child-static-tables-green.txt`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-child-static-tables-protocol-endpoint-green.txt`.
- Value: server tooling now parses the real `G7MTClient.exe` PE image, maps VA `0x007b6ae4` to the 18-dword P-array and VA `0x007b6ba8` to four 256-dword S-boxes, applies static table mask `xor 0x91`, and computes the child round helper `((S1[b2] + S0[b3]) xor S2[b1]) + S3[b0]`. Fixed vectors from the installed client include P-array head `25406b89 86a409d4 141a8b2f 04717445`, S-box0 head `d2320ca7 99e0b6ad 30fe73dc d11be0b8`, and round input `0x12345678 -> 0x3c71e1ca`.
- Interpretation: the server can now recover the static tables needed for the Blowfish-like child codec. The remaining gap is reproducing `0x613ad0` key schedule and full `0x614100`/`0x614460` block encode/decode.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms G005 C003 static table implementation progress; C001/C002 remain pending because no supported encrypted response has advanced the real client.

### 2026-06-09T13:55:00Z - G005 child codec key schedule and block codec

For real client tables and key `abcd`, scheduled P-array head is `57c3c24e 0761a8de 5aa506f6 57bed224`, scheduled S-box0 head is `2f12a783 badf4d3e c770046c 79117e9a`, zero-block encrypts to `(0x520b668b, 0x1a7badbd)`, and encoded `0011223344556677aa` is `b0d6bbbc98c7844c462bc9b51bae60df` with decoded padded plaintext `0011223344556677aa00000000000000`.
- Interpretation: raw child-codec encryption is now executable in server tooling. The next remaining gap is deriving/applying the actual phase key material from observed `0x0034`/phase1/phase2 flow and probing a real encrypted `0x0035` response.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms G005 C003 codec implementation progress; C001/C002 remain pending because no live client advancement has been proven.

### 2026-06-09T14:28:00Z - G005 configured encrypted phase3 response
- Source: `tools/logh7_phase3_response.py`, `src/server/logh7-server.mjs`, `tools/tests/test_logh7_cipher.py`, `tests/server/logh7-server.test.mjs`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-phase3-child-codec-response-tcp-surface.txt`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-phase3-child-codec-response-real-client-probe.qa.txt`.
- Value: server tooling now builds a full child-codec encrypted phase3 transport frame from decoded phase3 payload data. Fixed vector: static real-client tables + transport key `abcd` + phase3 payload `encipher_key=abcd`, `decipher_key=XY`, `sequence=1` yields frame `0012003503c1fac2922f89189de77564f80410f8`. The gameplay server emits this only when `server.gameplay.loginResponse` explicitly configures it, and TCP surface QA received the exact 20-byte frame with payload/response/close trace evidence.
- Interpretation: the server can now carry an evidence-backed encrypted `0x0035` candidate through its real TCP surface without changing the default no-fabrication policy. A real client probe with the `abcd` candidate still reports `[mpsCipherManager] exchange_key_phase3: param2 length is illegal(encipher)`, and that probe observed a different `0x0034` body (`d9f907a74bd30cc043f02db12b4a2b032961c0d2c4ff104d`) than earlier captures.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms configured encrypted response plumbing and refutes hard-coded `abcd` key material as sufficient for client advancement. C001/C002 remain pending; next work must derive per-run phase key material from the changing `0x0034` request/state instead of using a fixed key.

### 2026-06-09T15:15:00Z - G005 runtime key extraction dead ends
- Source: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-runtime-key-debug-probe-attach.stdout.txt`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-memory-key-scan-high.stdout.txt`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-runtime-key-probe-cleanup.txt`.
- Value: `DebugActiveProcess` attach produced `events=[]`, `exitProcess=true`; memory scan produced `keys=[]` before/after login while the server captured payload `001a003434fe1eaa3ddb5957b16e1d70dc6f9f452f9849ddd6930a27`; cleanup shows no game processes and `String.txt` size 927.
- Interpretation: debugger attach and naive heap vtable scan are not sufficient runtime key extraction methods. The next path should patch/log the key helper callsite or derive pointers from a live call path rather than object heap scanning.
- Refutes/Confirms: refutes the attach and heap-scan extraction methods; C001/C002 remain pending.

- Interpretation: the next non-debugger patch/log probe can now fail closed on PE signature drift before modifying a generated client binary.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms a safer path toward patch/log key extraction; C001/C002 remain pending until a real client probe advances or produces malformed encrypted-response edge evidence.

### 2026-06-09T23:35:00Z - G005 runtime probe plan
- Source: `tools/logh7_runtime_patch_targets.py`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g005-runtime-probe-plan-cli.json`.
- Value: probe plan found executable zero cave VA `0x0066acd5`, file offset `0x0026acd5`, length 811 bytes, plus IAT slots `CreateFileA=0x0066b1d0`, `WriteFile=0x0066b1c4`, `SetFilePointer=0x0066b2cc`, `CloseHandle=0x0066b1dc`, `OutputDebugStringA=0x0066b1c0`, `wsprintfA=0x0066b624`, `lstrlenA=0x0066b29c`.

- Refutes/Confirms: confirms the bounded candidate response set after decoded `0x0030`. Refutes guessing an arbitrary `0x0031` body or claiming lobby/login success before the payload schema is proven. C001/C002 remain pending because the client is not yet fully connected/playable.

Static disassembly confirmed both dispatchers load `esi = [head]` before reading `node+0x10`. The `RMN1` log has 16 records: flag-three first callback is always `0x004adf60`, while flag-zero first callback is `0x004ab6a0` six times and `0x004ac350` twice.
- Refutes/Confirms: refutes the assumption that observed zero-dispatcher entry directly invokes the `0x004adf60` setter with flag zero. Confirms current flag-three dispatch reaches `0x004adf60` but with literal flag `3`, while zero dispatch primarily enters a separate callback-list walker at `0x004ab6a0`. The next trace point is inside `0x004ab6a0` to identify nested callback pointers/flags or the state clear/follow-up path that prevents session/world state from persisting.

Verification: focused py_compile/unittest passed, `npm run test:tools` passed 134 tests, and `npm test` passed tools 134 + server 27 + Playwright 5.
- Interpretation: the client is not closing because the manager has already been destroyed; the cleanup entry sees a live runtime-manager global but the connection object is already in state `2` with no WSA error. The close is reached from the `0x00613150` branch after `call 0x00614bb0` and `call 0x00614b30`, so the next trace target is the event-loop/connection dispatcher around `0x00613150` and the two callees that decide the socket is complete/failed, not additional bootstrap/world response bodies.
- Refutes/Confirms: refutes the hypothesis that current candidates fail only after entering phase4/post-login recv or decoded-response promotion. Confirms the next protocol requirement is to keep the connection from being marked state `2`/cleanup before another receive is scheduled, or to discover the missing server response that makes the dispatcher choose the non-cleanup branch.

### 2026-06-10T09:20:00Z - G093 dispatcher cleanup-branch probe setup
- Hypotheses:
  1. The `0x00613150` branch is entered with the same connection pointer already carrying `state78=2`; distinguishing evidence is a pre-call record before `0x00614bb0` with `connectionThis`, `state78`, and dispatcher locals.
  2. `0x00614bb0` mutates the connection into cleanup state; distinguishing evidence is a post-call record whose `state78` or related members differ from the pre-call record.
  3. The branch is selected by dispatcher locals or saved registers rather than connection state; distinguishing evidence is stable connection fields but distinctive saved `ESI`/`EDI`/stack locals in the branch record.

- Source: `tools/logh7_socket_dispatcher_null_list_ring.py`, `tools/tests/test_logh7_socket_dispatcher_null_list_ring.py`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g114-baseline-null-list-ring-analysis.json`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g114-suppress-candidates-null-list-result.json`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g114-suppress-candidates-null-list-trace.jsonl`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g114-suppress-candidates-null-list-ring-analysis.json`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g114-echo0030-force0031-null-list-result.json`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g114-echo0030-force0031-null-list-trace.jsonl`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g114-echo0030-force0031-decipher-null-list-result.json`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g114-echo0030-force0031-decipher-null-list-trace.jsonl`.

- Value: Real-client QA with the same G095 patched EXE and `LOGH_SUPPRESS_CANDIDATES=1` sent only phase3 (`0x0035`) after the client `0x0034`; the client then emitted `0x0036` and `0x0030`. The trace later shows `ECONNRESET` when the harness killed the still-waiting client.

With `LOGH_RESPONSE_KEY=decipher`, the cipher stderr disappeared and the socket stayed open until harness timeout/reset, but no additional client packet arrived and the `SNL1` ring also stayed `counter=0`.
- Interpretation: H1 and H3 are confirmed; H2 is refuted for the observed run. Bare `0x0001/0x0003` at the current timing/encoding is a harmful route into stack-code-1 null-list cleanup and should not be treated as playable-session progress. The `0x0030` envelope route avoids that cleanup boundary, and decipher-key encoding is less wrong than phase1-key encoding for server-to-client `0x0030`, but the forced inner payload still does not advance the session. The next decisive probe should instrument the client's `0x0030` receive/parser path or response to the echoed `0x0030` body, not resume sending bare session/world transports.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms the immediate protocol direction is `0x0030` envelope/body semantics rather than raw `0x0001/0x0003/0x0013/0x0014`. Refutes using null-list cleanup as evidence of a missing robot setup trigger; G113 proved setup runs, and G114 proves the cleanup is caused by the current response-family experiment.

### 2026-06-10T11:05:00Z - G117 post-0x31 second-frame key transition
- Source: `tools/logh7_inner_0030_chain.py`, `tools/tests/test_logh7_inner_0030_chain.py`, `tools/logh7_world_init_probe_server.mjs`, `tests/server/logh7-world-init-probe-server.test.mjs`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g117-runtime-keysetup-log-cli.json`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g117-keysetup-result.json`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g117-keysetup-trace.jsonl`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g117-second-0030-gin7key-result.json`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g117-second-0030-gin7key-trace.jsonl`, `docs/logh7-0030-protocol.md`, `docs/playable-revival-policy.md`.

After accepted inner `0x31`, server-to-client `0x0030` frames must be encoded with the newly installed 37-byte GIN7 raw key, not the old `5859` decipher key. The next gate is no longer cipher selection; it is constructing a sufficiently long/typed post-key inner login/session OK body that satisfies the `mtNetStreamInputBuffer` reads and reaches enqueue/session flags.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms Claude's `0x004ad7e0` discovery is not the active blocker because G113 already proved the setup chain runs; confirms the post-`0x31` key transition as the current protocol boundary. Refutes reusing decipher key `5859` for chained post-key server frames.

### 2026-06-10T12:25:00Z - G119 post-key lobby parser and message-input probe
- Source: `tools/logh7_inner_0030_chain.py`, `tools/logh7_session_setup_trigger.py`, `tools/logh7_message_input_probe_patch.py`, `tools/tests/test_logh7_inner_0030_chain.py`, `tools/tests/test_logh7_session_setup_trigger.py`, `tools/tests/test_logh7_message_input_probe_patch.py`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g118-post-key-*.json`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g119-inner-0030-chain-current.json`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g119-session-setup-trigger-current.json`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g119-message-input-patch.json`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g119-test-tools.txt`.

- Hit-state result: clicking the top card (`650,315`) and bottom card (`650,480`) sampled UI hit records for active objects `0x13688ee4`, `0x13698064`, `0x13698f7c`, and `0x13699e94`; every sample still kept `objectFlagB00=0`, `objectFlagB02=0`, `objectFlagB10=0`, and no `0x2009` trace event was emitted.
- Interpretation: `id/status/name/description` are necessary-looking parser fields and now data-driven, but still not sufficient to arm state-`0x2a` card hit. The remaining gate is likely one of the nested `0x2004` blocks after parsed destination `+0xa8/+0x13c/+0x150/+0x2a0`, or a coupled `0x2006` record field used by the card-object builder. The next efficient probe is not more UI clicking; it is instrumenting the card builder / state-`0x2a` decision path to log which cached fields are tested before `FUN_005015f0` can set hit flags or before `FUN_0051bea0` sends `0x2009`.

### 2026-06-11T20:18:00+09:00 - G135 result: dynamic cards exist; per-object enable byte blocks selection

Disassembly showed a backward `jne`; the trampoline now uses short conditional pass-through plus rel32 jumps. Verified disassembly includes forward `je 0x66ace9`, `jmp 0x66adc5`, `jne 0x66acf5`, and `jmp 0x66adc5`.

Trace showed `0x2003 -> 0x2004`, then `0x2005(02) -> 0x2006`, then `0x2005(01) -> 0x2006`. The rendered card objects were present with valid geometry and ids: top card id `0x0112`, rect `152,103,408,142`; bottom card id `0x0113`, rect `152,268,408,142`; bottom/back control id `0x0114`, rect `250,423,209,50`.
- Blocking evidence: both dynamic card objects were active (`+0x08=1`) and input-marked (`+0x18=1`), but their per-object enable byte `+0x15` was `0`. The bottom/back control in the same screen had `+0x15=1`. Therefore `FUN_005015f0(mode=2)` rejects the cards before the later `+0xb00/+0xb02/+0xb10` hit-state bytes can matter.
- Live object dump: top card `0x1369e064` and bottom card `0x1369ef7c` both had `enabled15=0`, `pendingEnable16=0`, `savedEnable17=0`, `dwordCD0=2`, and all hit bytes zero. Control `0x1369fe94` had `enabled15=1`, `dwordCD0=2`. This rules out bad click coordinates and simple pending modal disable.
- Static follow-up: `FUN_005148b0` builds the card/control objects and initially calls `FUN_005024e0(...,1)`, while `FUN_00508930` can later enable/disable group/index objects from a data-array byte. Since the final card objects are disabled even though the builder enables them, a later updater is writing `+0x15=0`.
- Interpretation: cards are dynamic and the dynamic `0x2004` path is alive; the remaining server/protocol blocker is the data that lets the client keep card objects enabled. The next efficient probe is to hook `FUN_005024e0` or `FUN_00508930` and log object id/new enable value/return address for group1 ids `0x112/0x113/0x114`, rather than adding more UI click probes or hardcoding card objects.

### 2026-06-11T20:11:27+09:00 - G136 result: compact 0x2004 card gate enables top card and reaches 0x2009
- Source: `tools/logh7_object_enable_probe_patch.py`, `tools/tests/test_logh7_object_enable_probe_patch.py`, `src/server/logh7-login-protocol.mjs`, `tests/server/logh7-login-protocol.test.mjs`, `tests/server/logh7-login-session.test.mjs`, `.omo/ui-explorer/session-codex-card-enable-compact/`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g136-*.txt`, `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g136-compact-*.json`.
- RED/GREEN probe: added the guarded `FUN_005024e0` object-enable writer probe (`OEW1` ring). The first trampoline branch test failed because the null-object skip branch jumped past logging unconditionally; after the fix, disassembly showed `test edx,edx`, `jne log`, `jmp skip`, and `python -m unittest tools.tests.test_logh7_object_enable_probe_patch` passed. The hook logs return address, object pointer, new enable byte, flags `+0x08/+0x14/+0x15/+0x18`, object id `+0xb04`, and `+0xcd0`.
- Runtime writer proof: before the server fix, the card screen reached `0x2003 -> 0x2004` and rendered dynamic cards, but the enable ring showed top card id `0x0112` disabled by return address `0x0051f282` and bottom card id `0x0113` disabled by `0x0051f306`. Decompiling `FUN_0051f1c0` showed the top enable condition is `DAT_02216c8e in {1,2} && DAT_02216f28 == 2 && DAT_02216f29 != 0`; bottom uses the second record equivalents `DAT_02216ffa`, `DAT_02217294`, and `DAT_02217295`.
- Rejected hypothesis: writing bytes directly at `payload+0x2a0/+0x2a1` made the initial tests pass but failed in the real client. Live globals stayed `DAT_02216f28=0` and `DAT_02216f29=0`, and card click emitted no trace. This proved `0x2a0/+0x2a1` are parser destination fields, not wire-source offsets.
- Parser correction: `0x0043fd60` consumes the `0x2004` response as a compact sequential stream. After each record's counted name and description, the stream must still supply the zeroed `+0xa8` dword, two zeroed power blocks, `+0x13c` count, `+0x150` count, then card kind/count bytes that copy into destination `record+0x2a0/+0x2a1`. Because `+0x2a1=1` also causes one charged-character detail block to be consumed, records must be packed sequentially after the consumed bytes; source offset `index*0x36c` is wrong for the wire stream even though `0x36c` is the destination record stride.
- Server fix: `buildLobbyInformationCharacterChargeInner` now packs records sequentially from stream cursor `0x01`, emits status/name/description, skips the zeroed post-description prefix, writes card kind `2` and selectable/detail count `1`, then advances over one zero-filled charged-character detail block. Tests now assert first-record gates at stream `0x64/0x65`, second-record gates at `0xda/0xdb`, and that direct payload `0x2a0/0x2a1` remains zero.
- Real-client QA: with the compact stream fix, the card screen again requested `0x2003`, received `0x2004`, then requested both `0x2005` variants. Live globals changed to `top_a=02010000` and `top_b=01000000`; the enable ring showed top card id `0x0112` at return address `0x0051f282` with `newEnable=1`. Bottom stayed disabled because only one character record is currently emitted.
- Surface proof: clicking the enabled top card at window coordinates `650,315` emitted client inner `0x2009` (`innerPayloadHex=20090100`), and the server sent `0x200a` (`respLen=18`, `frameBytes=40`). The client then closed conn2, opened conn3, completed phase3, sent `0x0020` with payload `00000000`, and sent inner `0x0200` (`020047494e3700570000070069006e00650069003000300000`), which the current server still ignores.
- Verification: focused RED output saved at `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g136-compact-card-gate-red.txt`; focused GREEN output saved at `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g136-compact-card-gate-green.txt`. `npm run test:server` passed 65 tests (`.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g136-compact-test-server.txt`) and `npm run test:tools` passed 200 tests (`.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g136-compact-test-tools.txt`).
- Cleanup: `python -m tools.logh7_ui_explorer --session .omo/ui-explorer/session-codex-card-enable-compact stop` restored installed EXE SHA `2848be76a7662e25159353463bdfd8ff2f270ac5845ef4cea62983443c155345`; `.omo/work/logh7-installed/exe/G7MTClient.exe.uiexplorer` was absent. `netstat` showed only TIME_WAIT client endpoints for `:47900`, no LISTENING server.

### 2026-06-15 - G214 result: 0x1202 is not the character display-name source
- User correction: `content/roster/*` and AI-assisted roster/name maps are not original LOGH VII server data. They may be used only as synthetic payloads for field probing unless backed by shipped assets, client binary consumers, official documents, live memory, or TCP evidence.
- Static evidence: `FUN_004c1e80` copies 0x1202 rows from `payload+4` into `client+0x4c83a4`, stride `0x120`, with count at `client+0x4c83a0`. `FUN_0056a590` binds the info UI model to that table (`model+0x114 = client+0x4c83a4`, `model+0x118 = client+0x4c83a0`).
- Reader evidence: `FUN_00539ce0` walks the 0x1202 table by id at row `+0x00`, filter byte at `+0x4c`, nested count at `+0x74`, and nested entries around `+0x78/+0x7c` with stride `0x28`. The decompiler made a misleading call shape; disassembly shows the row id is pushed into `FUN_004b4b60` through the manager returned by `FUN_004b5b80`, so 0x1202 is a candidate/filter table, not the display-name record.
- Root cause of blank names: the attempted server-side 0x1202 `displayName` mirroring was a guessed packed 0x0323 layout and was live-refuted. It can also corrupt 0x1202 filter/nested fields. The name path to pursue is the full 0x0323 record, whose parser/debug dumper (`FUN_00419300`) documents `parentage_len@0x7d`, `parentage[0].truth@0x80`, and `display_name@0xb8/0xba`.
- Implementation direction: stop synthesizing 0x1202 name fields. Populate 0x0323 parentage count/truth/display_name only when a name/rank/face sub-record is present, and treat any current name string as provisional display data unless separately proven original.

### 2026-06-16 - G217 result: live five-phase 0x1008 now commits one character, but post-create queue still stops after 0x031d
- Source: `src/server/logh7-login-session.mjs`, `tests/server/logh7-login-session.test.mjs`, `.omo/ui-explorer/session-charcreate-fix-20260616/trace.jsonl`, `.omo/ulw-loop/full-revival-20260615/evidence/postcreate-trace-compare.json`, `.omo/ulw-loop/full-revival-20260615/evidence/postcreate-1008-fix-summary.json`, `.omo/ulw-loop/full-revival-20260615/evidence/dispatch-004ba2b0-create-stall.txt`.
- RED proof: replaying the live five `0x1008` phases against the old session handler registered phase `0`, `2`, `3`, and `4` as independent new characters. The later `0x2003` card-list path then failed with `invalid lobby character-charge record count: 4`, proving the live phases are one multi-step create transaction rather than four creates.
- Server fix: `CommandGenerateCharacterCharge 0x1008` phase `0` now creates one draft character and phases `1..4` echo the same draft id/status without appending to `lobbyCharacters`; final phase `4` commits `generatedCharacterId`. World-entry id selection now prefers `chargedCharacterId || generatedCharacterId || LOGH_WORLD_CHAR_ID`, so the newly-created character id is used for `LOGH_WORLD_PUSH` and `0x0f02 -> 0x0204`.
- Regression coverage: added `LIVE_MULTIPHASE_CREATE_HEX` and `login session commits the live five-phase 0x1008 create only once and uses it for world entry`. The test asserts the five live frames produce exactly one `0x2004` card and that `0x0f02` returns the created id. Focused test passed after the fix; `npm run test:server` passed `660/660`.
- Full-suite verification: `npm test` passed after updating the `test_logh7_real_client_probe.py` fake Win32 surface to match the existing absolute-move click helper (`GetSystemMetrics`, `MOUSEEVENTF_MOVE`, `MOUSEEVENTF_ABSOLUTE`). Final counts: tools `223/223`, server `660/660`, Playwright `5/5`.

### 2026-06-16 - G222 result: 0x0315 grid parser byte-order fixed; C001 moves to post-render/object promotion
- Source: `src/server/logh7-login-protocol.mjs`, `tests/server/logh7-login-protocol.test.mjs`, `tests/server/logh7-login-session.test.mjs`, `.omo/ulw-loop/full-revival-20260615/evidence/c001-g222-playable-ringclear-gate-summary.json`, `c001-g222-mob0315-ring.json`, `c001-g222-be-ringclear-gate-summary.json`, `c001-g222-be-ringclear-stop.json`, and `.omo/ui-explorer/session-c001-g222-be-ringclear-live/trace.jsonl`.
- Patch-base control: rebuilt `.omo/work/marker-fix/G7MTClient.playable.earlygrid-ringclear.exe` from the current playable client plus `earlygrid-ringclear.codepage_patch.json` (SHA `e75486ef762787448d91e38a612103f6d11691833c36a6bcb30d13a9cbdb2366`). A pre-fix live run with the P15 gate probe still stopped at `0x0314->0x0315`: `dispatcher-0315-grid-arm-004bae19=0`, `dispatcher-0315-after-ring-clear=0`, `dispatcher-0313=0`, `stageMarkerRange=0`, `liveClass3=0`, and `markerValid=0`. This refuted patch-base mismatch and showed ringclear alone was not the missing marker fix.
- Message-object proof before the server fix: a temporary `MOB1` probe filtered to app code `0x0315` recorded `counter=2`, `sitesSeen=["lookupResult","inputBefore"]`, `resultAl=1`, `streamLen=5010`, `appCodeHex=0x0315`, and `inputMethodHex=0x004134e0`, with no `inputAfter` or handler. So the response reached `FUN_00404610` and then stopped inside the `0x004134e0` StaticInformationGrid parser.
- Static parser root cause: `FUN_004134e0` reads `[u8 width][u8 height]`, then helper-reads a u16 at payload `+2` and rejects values `>=0x1389`. The old server wrote `pairs.length` little-endian. For the real galaxy grid this made the helper see `0x4601` (=17921), tripping the count gate before dispatcher case `0x0315`; empty/fleet test grids similarly decoded as swapped counts (`0x2800`, `0x2a00`). `FUN_004abbb0` later reads the parsed buffer host-order, so the wire must be BE into the helper even though the downstream buffer is host-order.
- Server fix: `buildStaticInformationGridInner` now writes `rleByteCount` with `payload.writeUInt16BE(pairs.length, 2)`, and tests decode/assert that field as BE. Comments and `docs/logh7-strategic-map-wire.md` were updated to describe the count as RLE byte length, not pair count.
- Regression evidence: changing the tests to BE first failed against the old builder (`512 !== 2` / out-of-range decode), then the builder fix made the focused `StaticInformationGrid|0x0314 RequestStaticInformationGrid|StrategicGalaxyGrid|places a fleet cell` run pass (`99/99`). `node --check` passed for the changed source/test files.
- Live after the fix: the same playable ringclear client plus P15 gate probe no longer stalled at the parser. The probe captured `dispatcher-0315-grid-arm-004bae19=2`, `dispatcher-0315-after-ring-clear-004bae21=2`, `dispatcher-0313-gridtype-arm-004bae37=2`, `FUN_004c2a30-world-reset-promote` enter/leave, `FUN_004c5350-staging-to-live` enter/leave, `FUN_004d3bd0-marker-render-build` enter/leave, and `FUN_004b64c0-scene-build` enter/leave. Max observed state included `walkState=16`, `mode=2`, `stageNonzero=3781`, `stageMarkerRange=1018`, `liveNonzero=81`, `liveMarkerRange=81`, `snapshotGuard=1`, and `snapshotReady=1`.
- Remaining blocker: C001 still does not pass. The trace reached `0x0f02`, then extra `0x0313`, `0x0315`, `0x0325`, `0x0323`, and `0x0f03`, but the client closed with `read ECONNRESET` after `0x0f03`; no `0x0f06`/HUD/clickable-marker result was observed in this patched live run. The marker/render samples still had `stageClass3=0`, `liveClass3=0`, and `markerValid=0`. The next target is object-table promotion/sample-offset correctness or the post-render/post-`0x0f03` termination path, not the `0x0315` count/parser.
- Cleanup: `.omo/ulw-loop/full-revival-20260615/evidence/c001-g222-be-ringclear-stop.json` restored installed EXE SHA `2848be76a7662e25159353463bdfd8ff2f270ac5845ef4cea62983443c155345` with `shaVerified=true`; `c001-g222-be-ringclear-cleanup-check.json` recorded no remaining game processes or listeners on `4787`, `47900`, or `47901`.

### 2026-06-16 - G223 setup: normal playable early-grid discriminator after BE 0x0315 fix
- Goal: distinguish whether the G222 post-`0x0f03` close is caused by the `earlygrid-ringclear` client patch path, by remaining 0x0313/0x0315 object-table promotion/sample-offset ambiguity, or by a still-live early real-grid walk stall now that the `0x0315` RLE byte count is BE.
- References used: durable ULW plan `.omo/ulw-loop/full-revival-20260615/goals.json`, latest C001 artifacts (`c001-g222-be-ringclear-gate-summary.json`, G221 live-state/player-info/selector probes), `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF-2026-06-16.md` as older context only, `src/server/logh7-login-session.mjs`, and existing read-only `.omo/work/probe_marker_gate.py`.
- Hypotheses:
  1. H1 patch/timing artifact: G222's close after `0x0f03` is specific to `.omo/work/marker-fix/G7MTClient.playable.earlygrid-ringclear.exe`; the normal playable client with the BE server fix can continue to `0x0f06`/HUD even with `LOGH_STRAT_GRID_EARLY=1`. Distinguishing evidence: trace contains `0x0f06->0x0f07` and UI reaches HUD.
  2. H2 early real-grid still stalls: the `LOGH_STRAT_GRID_EARLY=1` path remains incompatible with the world-init walk despite the BE parser fix. Distinguishing evidence: trace stops after `0x0314->0x0315` or before `0x0f02`, matching G210b but now with BE wire.
  3. H3 object-table interpretation/offset issue: real 0x0313/0x0315 reaches dispatcher and stage/live cell grids, but class-3 samples remain zero only because the probe or current table offset is wrong. Distinguishing evidence: `probe_marker_gate.py` shows nonzero class3 in either `stageAt3f57d4`, `stageAfterLead`, `liveAt2c1754`, or `liveAt2c1755`, and the raw cell marker values correlate with those IDs.
  4. H4 true object promotion blocker: stage/live cells carry marker-range values but both object-table interpretations stay class3=0, so the marker render table cannot build valid clickable records. Distinguishing evidence: gate probe records dispatcher/render entries plus `markerTable.valid=0` and all class3 counts zero.

### 2026-06-16 - G224 setup: instrument 0x0313 message-object path
- Goal: determine whether `0x0313 ResponseStaticInformationGridType` reaches `FUN_00404610` as a raw-copy message object, which input method handles it, and whether it returns/dispatches normally before `FUN_004ba2b0 case 0x313` copies the record.
- Static setup evidence: `FUN_004ba2b0 case 0x313` bulk-copies 0x4b dwords + 1 byte from `param_3` to `clientBase+0x3f57d4`; the adjacent `FUN_004131e0` decompile looks like a grid-type parser but appears to parse text/CSV-style input rather than a raw message32 stream. Dynamic evidence is needed before changing server bytes.
- Hypotheses:
  1. H1 raw-copy path: `0x0313` uses a pass-through message object and returns to the dispatcher; the server's object payload is copied as-is, so the class3=1 observation means the server's emitted 0x0313 payload is already wrong at runtime or later overwritten.
  2. H2 parser-transform path: `0x0313` enters an input method that transforms or bounds the payload differently than the current 301-byte lead+records assumption. Distinguishing evidence: MOB1 ring shows a concrete input method and lack of handler/normal return or unexpected stream length.
  3. H3 correct 0x0313 admission but wrong object offset: the payload is accepted and copied, but `FUN_004d3bd0` reads a different base/stride than current probes assume. Distinguishing evidence: MOB1 returns normally while raw staged bytes correlate with intended records at a shifted offset.
  4. H4 content lookup veto: class3 records exist but marker table stays empty because byte0/content-table lookup fails before the marker record is marked valid. Distinguishing evidence would require later `FUN_004d3bd0` branch probes, after H1-H3 are settled.

### 2026-06-16 - G224 result: 0x0313 first byte is count, not lead; server builder fixed
- Source: `.omo/ulw-loop/full-revival-20260615/evidence/c001-g224-mob0313-ring-retry.json`, `c001-g224-object-table-memory.json`, `c001-g224-func-00413050.txt`, `src/server/logh7-login-protocol.mjs`, `tests/server/logh7-login-protocol.test.mjs`, and `tests/server/logh7-login-session.test.mjs`.
- Live MOB1 outcome: the first G224 attempt did not reach world-init, so the ring was empty. The retry reached the full path (`0x0312->0x0313`, `0x0314->0x0315`, `0x0f02`, `0x0f06`, grid-enter). The filtered `0x0313` ring recorded `inputBefore`, `inputAfter`, `handlerBefore`, and `handlerAfter`, verdict `handler returned`; input method is `0x00413050`, stream length `5010`, handler method `0x004a9cf0`.
- Static parser root cause: `FUN_00413050` calls the stream helper at vtbl+0x24, then reads `*param_1` as a count and requires `<0x65`; for each entry it helper-reads three single bytes into `param_1[1+i*3..3+i*3]`. The old server wrote byte 0 as an unused lead byte (0), so the client parsed count=0 and left the object records zero. This directly explains G223's `stageAt3f57d4Class3=0` and `markerTable.valid=0` even when the live cell grid had 81 marker-range values.
- Runtime memory confirmation before the fix: after the G224 retry, `c001-g224-object-table-memory.json` showed stage `0x3f57d4` first 128 bytes all zero and no class3 records at offsets 0/1/2. Live `0x2c1754` had only one stale/misaligned class3 record. That is consistent with count=0 parser output, not with a valid 81-object table.
- Server fix: `buildStaticInformationGridTypeInner` now sets `payload[0] = maxObjectValue + 1` and still lays records at `1 + value*3`, preserving cell value `v -> objectTable[v]` by including zero filler records for unused lower values. Tests now assert the count for single fleet, projected systems, fleet+systems, capped galaxy, and login-session `0x0f02`/`0x0312` paths.
- Regression evidence: `node --check` passed for `src/server/logh7-login-protocol.mjs`, `tests/server/logh7-login-protocol.test.mjs`, and `tests/server/logh7-login-session.test.mjs`; focused protocol/session tests for grid type / strategic galaxy / early grid passed (`44/44` and `55/55` in the filtered runs).
- Cleanup: `c001-g224-mob0313-cleanup.json` records `shaVerified=true` and ports `4787`, `47900`, and `47901` closed after stopping `.omo/ui-explorer/session-c001-g224-mob0313`.

### 2026-06-16 - G238 setup: command-row factory dispatch census
- Goal: determine whether tested C001 clicks reach the command factory dispatcher `FUN_004f93c0`, and if so whether the selected factory index is SelectGrid (`0x2b`) or some other command/status.
- Static setup evidence:
  - `FUN_004f93c0(param_1,param_2,param_3)` is the factory dispatcher: if `*(code **)(param_1 + param_2*4 + 0x1c)` is non-null, it calls that factory, stores `param_2` at the new dialog object's `+0x28`, and links the object into the manager list. For SelectGrid, `param_2` must be `0x2b`, whose handler table slot is `_DAT_00c9e3a8 = FUN_00581c80`.
  - The only decompiled caller is `FUN_004f58c0`. It iterates hit-tested command rows (`FUN_005015f0(2, rowPtr, ...)`) and reads the selected u16 command/factory index from `FUN_004c8700() + category*0x46 + 0x20 + selectedIndex*2`, where `FUN_004c8700()` is `clientBase+0x3416d8` when its guard byte is non-zero.
  - `FUN_005321a0` and `FUN_00579800` rebuild/classify the command row state. Relevant fields: `param_1+0xb28` row count, `+0xb2c` selected row, `+0x234` mode/state, `+0x1580` status classification, global `DAT_00c9eabc` selected index, and global `DAT_00c9eac0` category.
- Hypotheses:
  1. H1 row-hit gate: tested clicks never enter `FUN_004f58c0` with a hit, so `FUN_004f93c0` stays at `0`. Next target is UI hitbox/list population.
  2. H2 wrong factory index: `FUN_004f93c0` fires, but `param_2 != 0x2b`. Next target is the static command table (`0x0307`/card-command data) or selected category/index.
  3. H3 SelectGrid factory pointer missing/null: `FUN_004f93c0(param_2=0x2b)` fires but the factory pointer is null or not `FUN_00581c80`. Next target is handler-table initialization/manager object setup.
  4. H4 positive control: `FUN_004f93c0(param_2=0x2b)` and `FUN_00581c80` fire for one input, shifting the blocker back into SelectGrid/command gate with concrete coordinates.

H1 command-activation data gap: the strategic command path is still blocked because the client-side current-character/actionability payload lacks a proven category/room/context entry that triggers `FUN_004f6b00 -> FUN_004f5cb0 -> FUN_004f58c0 -> FUN_004f93c0(0x2b)`. Distinguishing evidence: static XREFs from `0x0f08`, `0x0356`, `0x0321`, and institution/room handlers show which payload populates `*(DAT_007ccffc+8)+0x270`, `HUD+0xab0`, category `D6`, or the `0x3579d0` command/result table.
  2. H2 world-position data gap: current server data knows names/orbits but not the original strategic coordinates. Distinguishing evidence: content and decompiled parsers show no field path from `content/galaxy.json` rect/cx/cy or model star nodes into `0x0313/0x0315/0x031d/0x0f02` server responses; if true, next fix is data extraction/mapping, not command code.
  3. H3 institution/room data gap: office/room surfaces are separate `institution`/`room` read-models or command contexts not wired into the current server. Distinguishing evidence: client strings/tokens contain `$xinstitution$`, `$yinstitution$`, room references, and `0x0321` parser structure, but current content source lacks concrete room/office positions and room-to-character context.
  4. H4 observability/version gap: a field is already present in existing files but not carried into the live path because the adapter drops it, a gate flag suppresses it, or the live client uses a different object than the one probed. Distinguishing evidence: static code/data inventory finds candidate fields but server wire dumps and live memory summaries show they are absent after parse.

  7 face TCF atlases, 1355 `tcf.hed` entries, and 416 decodable portrait slots.

  default base catalog; active installed CP949 MsgDat is quarantined as localization evidence only.

  `content/client/msgdat.json` for default catalog ids. `characterDisplayName()` no longer prefers Korean/IV EX
  fields, and the VII `characters` DB table no longer imports IV EX `name_kr`/`iv_id` into default character rows
  (the separate `ivex_*` reference tables remain separate reference data).

### 2026-06-16 - G246 correction/result: current location fields added; marker/planet claims narrowed; Empire fief system confirmed
- Source: user correction after G245, `src/server/logh7-login-session.mjs`, `src/server/logh7-login-protocol.mjs`,
  `docs/logh7-info-records-wire.md`, `content/manual/strategy-commands.json`, `content/extracted/dat-tables.json`,
  `content/manual/org-posts.json`, and registry-confirmed install root
  `HKCU:\SOFTWARE\BOTHTEC\銀河英雄伝説VII\1.0 Install=E:\logh7-revival\.omo\work\logh7-installed`.
- Marker correction: G245's "strategic markers/labels" language was too strong. The proven server/client fact is
  class-3 marker slot/cell population through `0x0313/0x0315`. Current system marker `byte0` remains
  `index & 0xff`, not the real one-byte group-0x18 label/link id; current `byte2` is a faction tint, not recovered
  star/fortress/black-hole type. System names match `constmsg.dat` records, but ids are 1406..2844, so they cannot
  be written directly into the one-byte `0x0313` content id. Planet data is catalogued (80 systems / 281 planets),
  not wired into stable selected-system planet render.
- Current-location code change: added server-authored location fields for the player downlink. `0x0323` now carries
  `spot@0x1c` and `spot_owner@0x20`; `0x0325` full unit records now carry `commander@+0x08`, strategic
  `cell@+0x0c`, `owner@+0x10`, and `mapSection@+0x48`. Sources are `LOGH_WORLD_SPOT_ID` / `LOGH_WORLD_SPOT_OWNER`
  and `LOGH_FLEET_ROW * 100 + LOGH_FLEET_COL`, with defaults spot 1, owner 1, fleet cell 2550. This fixes server
  downlink consistency, but remains authored seed data rather than recovered original starting position/state.
- Position/post status: rank is a character field (`0x1008 rank` on create, `0x0323` parentage `rank@0xd6` on
  render). Duty/post state is the seat array (`seatCount@0x250`, seat entries `{character, role}` at `0x254`) and
  personnel commands such as `0x0707 CardAppointment` (`seat_role@0x1c`, `chief_spot@0x20`). Manual org data has
  58 Empire posts and 63 Alliance posts, but original post occupancy and role enum names are not recovered.
- Create-character seed status: the current server stores new id/status, card/full names, power/blood/sex, face,
  resolved ability seed, bonus/title/rank, and current spot/owner. The packed parser currently does not persist
  `flagship_type`, `flagship_kind`, or `flagship_name`; later 0x1008 create phases are accepted by draft id/status
  but still need capture for full semantics.
- Empire fief/nobility discriminator: the system is present in installed/base data. Manual strategy commands include
  `叙爵` (index 48), `封土授与` (53), `封土直轄` (54), and `狩猟` (56, invited hunting at a mansion on one's own
  fief planet). Extracted base strings include noble titles (`公爵`, `侯爵`, `伯爵`, `子爵`, `男爵`), `爵位`,
  `封土`, central/local tax labels, and text stating fief tax belongs to the lord. Server still lacks the
  authoritative fief ownership table and live command/apply loop, so this is confirmed design/data, not playable yet.
- Verification so far: added a failing test for current-location fields in the 0x0f02 player spawn, then made it
  pass. `node --test --test-name-pattern "current location fields" tests/server/logh7-login-session.test.mjs`
  passed, and full `node --test tests/server/logh7-login-session.test.mjs` passed (`60` tests, `0` failures).
- Additional verification: `node --check src/server/logh7-login-session.mjs` passed. Focused
  `node --test tests/server/logh7-login-session.test.mjs tests/server/logh7-login-protocol.test.mjs` passed
  (`105` tests, `0` failures). Full `npm run test:server` passed (`667` tests, `0` failures).

### 2026-06-16 - G255 result: strategic marker snapshot fixed by preloading 0x0313 before 0x0314
- Root cause narrowed: the client world-init walk requests `0x0314` (cell grid) before `0x0312` (object table). A real
  early `0x0315` can therefore be snapshotted with stale object-table data, leaving server cells in live memory but
  too few class-3 objects for marker rendering/selection.
- Server fix: when `LOGH_STRAT_GRID_EARLY=1` and `LOGH_STRAT_GALAXY=1`, `0x0304 -> 0x0305` now preloads the
  strategic object table as an extra `0x0313` before the first `0x0314 -> 0x0315`. `LOGH_STRAT_GRID_OBJECT_PRELOAD=0`
  disables this paired preload if a future discriminator needs the old behavior.
- Live proof: `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-object-preload-47900-20260617` used the canonical playable EXE
  SHA `1f7fad439af2fc7f775b4cdfb2a8e10111ebd5209f98dab8905c9b3b238cc00c` and reached world/HUD. Trace order:
  `0x0304 -> 0x0305`, extra `0x0313`, then `0x0314 -> 0x0315`, `0x0312 -> 0x0313`, full `0x0f02` world-init,
  and post-load `0x0f06 -> 0x0f07` plus `0x0b09/0x0325/0x0323/0x0b0a/0x0356/0x1200/0x1202/0x1201/0x0305/0x0307`.
- Frida marker gate proof: `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-object-preload-47900-20260617/marker-gate-preload.jsonl`
  recorded `stageMarkerRange=81`, `liveMarkerRange=81`, `stageClass3=81`, `liveClass3=81`, and
  `markerTable.valid=81` with mode `2`, built flag `0x35837f=1`, and snapshot guard/ready both `1`.
- Remaining blocker: grid/map clicks still emitted no inbound `0x0b01` and no outbound `0x0b07`; movement is still
  blocked upstream in command/actionability activation, not in the strategic marker render table. The lower-left HUD
  text remains the separate non-GDI renderer/source problem from G254.

### 2026-06-17 - G256 setup: action-list category seed for SelectGrid activation
- Goal: test whether the populated 0x0356 action-list payload must carry a command category value rather than the
  active character id. G241 proved the 0x0356 count reaches `PLAYER_INFO+0x270`, but `listSelected189=-1`,
  `categoryResolve=0`, and no `0x0b01/0x0b07` followed. G238 proved category `0`, row `4` maps to SelectGrid
  factory `0x2b` in the live command table.
- Static discriminator: `FUN_004f6b00` resolves the category from `payload + (count - selected) * 8 + 0x26c`.
  For one selected action-list row this reads the first 16 bits of `PLAYER_INFO+0x274`, which `FUN_004c0400`
  copies from 0x0356 body `+0x254`. Therefore the server must be able to seed that value explicitly.
- Server test/setup: added opt-in `LOGH_ACTION_LIST_CATEGORY=<0..65535>`, which makes the active action-list entry
  write `{ character: category, role: 0 }` instead of overloading the active character id. Focused unit checks passed:
  `node --check src/server/logh7-login-session.mjs` and
  `node --test --test-name-pattern "action-list category zero|post-load 0x0f06|duty card command" tests/server/logh7-login-session.test.mjs`
  (`4` tests, `0` failures).
- Hypotheses:
  1. H1 correct category seed: with `LOGH_ACTION_LIST_CATEGORY=0`, selecting the post-load action-list row causes
     `FUN_004f6b00 -> FUN_004f5cb0(0)`, command row 4 maps to `0x2b`, and SelectGrid or `0x0b01` appears.
  2. H2 UI selection still missing: the list is populated but tested clicks leave `listSelected189=-1` and
     `categoryResolve=0`; next target is selection-list hit coordinates or mode gate.
  3. H3 category seed insufficient: category applies but row hit/factory dispatch still stays zero; next target is
     command-row geometry/status classification, not 0x0356 payload bytes.
- Artifacts:
  - [ ] `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g256-action-category-*` - live UI explorer session, screenshots, trace.
  - [ ] `.omo/ulw-loop/full-revival-20260615/evidence/g256-action-category/` - Frida log/summary and cleanup receipt.

     show hit-test true events but `listSelected189=-1`, `HUD+0xab0=-1`, and no `hud-frame-selection-change`.
  3. H3 category/menu gate: selection changes, but `FUN_004f6b00` resolves `-1` or `FUN_004f5cb0` never applies a
     category with row `0x2b` SelectGrid. Distinguishing evidence: category/row/factory hook logs show resolver or
     command row failure after selection.
- Artifacts to revert/cleanup:
  - [ ] `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g257-action-hook-le-20260617/` - live real-client session. Cleanup:
    `python -m tools.logh7_ui_explorer --session .omo/ui-explorer/session-g257-action-hook-le-20260617 stop`.

### 2026-06-17 - G257 result: synthetic category-0 action seat is not enough for live command activation
- Baseline live session `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g257-action-hook-le-20260617` with default LE `0x0325`,
  early grid/galaxy/grid-enter, and the G256 action hooks reached the strategic HUD but had no selectable command
  payload: server/runtime evidence stayed at `recordSeatCount250=0`, `payloadCount270=0`, `listCount188=0`, and no
  inbound `0x0b01` or outbound `0x0b07`.
- Category probe sessions `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g257b-action-category-le-20260617` and
  `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g257c-g241-category-20260617` enabled `LOGH_POSTLOAD_RICH_CHARACTER=1`,
  `LOGH_ACTION_LIST_CATEGORY=0`, and the strategic/tactics bundles. The server trace wrote the post-load action
  seat fields with `recordSeatCount250=1`, but when the first dword was exactly zero the Frida dispatcher/tray hooks
  still observed `notifySeatCount250=0`, `liveSeatCount270=0`, `payloadCount270=0`, and `listCount188=0`. This refuted
  raw zero as a valid carrier for category 0 through the native client parser.
- Fix/probe applied: `activeSeatEntries()` now encodes category 0 as dword `0x00010000`, keeping the low u16 category
  value at zero while avoiding an all-zero first dword. Regression tests now assert this on both the full
  `0x0323` character record and the `0x0356` post-load character delta.
- Live refutation: `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g257d-sentinel-category-20260617` sent both early `0x0323` and post-load
  `0x0356` with `recordSeatCount250=1`, `recordSeatChar254=65536`, and `recordSeatRole258=0`, but the real client still
  reached `dispatcher-0356-enter` and `strategy-tray-update-enter` with `notifySeatCount250=0`,
  `notifySeatChar254=0`, `liveSeatCount270=0`, `listCount188=0`, and `payloadCount270=0`. The sentinel therefore
  documents the wire/layout hypothesis, but it is not sufficient to activate command interaction in the live client.
- Interpretation: command activation likely requires a real validated duty-card/seat object relationship rather than
  a synthetic category dword in the character delta. The next reverse-engineering target is the `0x0356` native
  parser/validator path and the exact G241-style duty-card payload that previously populated nonzero action-list
  fields, then mapping how that payload sets `PLAYER_INFO+0x270/+0x274`.
- Verification: `node --check src/server/logh7-login-session.mjs`,
  `node --test --test-name-pattern "action-list category zero|post-load 0x0f06" tests/server/logh7-login-session.test.mjs`,
  and `npm run test:server` all passed. The full server suite reported `684` passing tests and `0` failures.
- Cleanup: stopped `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g257d-sentinel-category-20260617`, verified the canonical playable EXE SHA
  restored to `1f7fad439af2fc7f775b4cdfb2a8e10111ebd5209f98dab8905c9b3b238cc00c`, and killed Frida driver PID `50548`
  plus its child processes.

### 2026-06-17 - G006 P0-02 live coordinate/render verification setup
- 목표: 데이터를 새로 만들기 전에 현재 서버가 보내는 `0x0313` object table, `0x0315` sector grid,
  staging/live promotion, marker render table, screenshot marker 위치가 같은 성계/요새/행성 후보를
  가리키는지 실제 `G7MTClient.exe`에서 검증한다. 이번 라운드는 좌표를 원본 권위 데이터로 확정하지 않고,
  `content/galaxy.json` manual projection 및 current-source wire가 서로 섞이는지 여부만 판정한다.
- 가설:
  1. H1 wire/projection 일치: `0x0313.byte0`이 constmsg group `0x18` sub-id를 싣고, `0x0315`
     cell value가 같은 object value를 가리키며, render marker와 screenshot label/info panel이 같은
     대상이다. 구분 증거: trace/object dump, live table dump, screenshot/info panel target이 모두 일치한다.
  2. H2 ID 공간 혼합: `MsgDat` 큰 record id와 `0x0313.byte0` one-byte sub-id가 다시 섞여 label 또는
     info panel이 다른 성계를 가리킨다. 구분 증거: wire byte0이 `docs/logh7-world-data-mining-status.md`
     의 `constmsg` group `0x18` sub-id와 다르거나, screenshot label이 expected target과 다르다.
  3. H3 좌표 투영/격자 변환 문제: byte0/name은 맞지만 `cx/cy -> 100x50` projection 또는 collision
     nudge가 문서 좌표와 달라 screenshot상 위치가 다르다. 구분 증거: object/cell id와 marker label은
     맞고, cell-to-screen mapping만 예상과 어긋난다.
  4. H4 promotion/timing 문제: 서버 trace에는 최신 `0x0313/0x0315`가 있으나 client live table은 이전
     empty/stale snapshot을 유지한다. 구분 증거: staging에는 marker가 있으나 live table 또는 marker
     render table이 0/old value다.

  - `python -m tools.logh7_ui_explorer stop`으로 이전 세션을 정리하고 canonical playable SHA
    `1f7fad439af2fc7f775b4cdfb2a8e10111ebd5209f98dab8905c9b3b238cc00c` 복구를 확인한다.
  - safe full-world env만 사용한다. `LOGH_DUTY_CARDS=1`, `LOGH_ROSTER_PUSH=1`,
    `LOGH_STRAT_GRID_EARLY=1` 같은 금지 기본 플래그는 좌표 검증 런에서 켜지 않는다.

### 2026-06-17 - G006 C002: 범주 0 재타깃 실클라 계측
- 목적: `0x0305/0x0307` 직무카드 가설을 철회한 뒤, `LOGH_ACTION_LIST_CATEGORY=0`만 켠 상태에서
  실제 `G7MTClient.exe`가 선택 행을 범주 0으로 해석하고 명령 메뉴를 여는지 확인한다.
- 환경: `tools.logh7_ui_explorer` 세션
  `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-category0-retarget-20260617`, canonical playable SHA
  `1f7fad439af2fc7f775b4cdfb2a8e10111ebd5209f98dab8905c9b3b238cc00c`, 서버 PID `38864`,
  클라이언트 PID `8896`.
- 금지 플래그 확인: `LOGH_DUTY_CARDS`, `LOGH_NPC_AI`, `LOGH_RELAY`, `LOGH_AUTHORITATIVE`,
  `LOGH_ROSTER_PUSH`, `LOGH_STRAT_GRID_EARLY`는 effective LOGH env에 없음.
- 되돌릴/정리할 산출물: 세션 종료는
  `python -m tools.logh7_ui_explorer --session .omo\ui-explorer\session-g006-category0-retarget-20260617 stop`.
  Frida 로그 프로세스는 실행 후 종료 확인이 필요하며, 포트 `47900`과 게임/Frida 프로세스가 비어야 한다.
- 가설:
  1. [검증중] 클릭 좌표/모드가 이전 세션과 달라 선택 row hit가 나지 않는다. 구분 증거:
     `target-global-rect`, `list-selection-change`, `hud.modeF4` 변화.
  2. [검증중] 선택 payload의 first entry가 명령 범주 0으로 유지되지 않고 character/card id로 정규화된다. 구분 증거:
     `category-resolve.retval`, `list.firstEntryWord274`, `list.wouldResolveCategory`.
  3. [검증중] 범주 0은 해석되지만 static command table이 비어 `FUN_004f5cb0(0)`이 row를 만들지 않는다.
     구분 증거: `category-apply.after.rowCountD4`, `factory-dispatch`, `menu-row-hit`.
- 1차 관측: category-only 세션은 `0x0323` fixed record의 seat char를 `65536`으로 보냈지만,
  compact `0x0356` trace와 Frida 선택 payload는 `recordSeatChar254=0`, `firstEntryWord274=0`,
  `firstEntryDword274=0`이었다. 모드 클릭 뒤 `modeF4=2`, list row hit-test true까지는 갔지만
  `list-selection-change`, `category-resolve`, `category-apply`, `factory-dispatch`는 없었다.
- 추가 비교 산출물: appointment 경유 세션
  `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-category0-appointment-20260617`을 생성해
  `LOGH_ACTION_LIST_APPOINTMENT=1`이 `0x0707` apply로 payload entry를 채우는지 본다.
  정리 명령은 `python -m tools.logh7_ui_explorer --session .omo\ui-explorer\session-g006-category0-appointment-20260617 stop`.
- 2차 관측: appointment 세션 trace에는 `0x0707`이 전송됐지만, attach가 `0x0707` 이후라 적용 호출은 놓쳤다.
  초기 post-apply 스냅샷도 `firstEntryWord274=0`, `firstEntryDword274=0`으로 유지됐다.
  다음 세션 `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-category0-appointment-apply-20260617`은 캐릭터 선택 전
  `g006-c002-card-appointment-apply-probe-20260617.js`를 먼저 붙여 `dispatcher-0707-enter`,
  `find-unit-*`, `appointment-apply-*`를 잡는다.
- 3차 관측: 적용 훅을 먼저 붙인 세션에서 서버 trace는 `0x0707`을 보냈지만
  `dispatcher-0707-enter`, `find-unit-*`, `appointment-apply-*` 이벤트가 전혀 없었다. 현재 S→C
  `0x0707` 주입은 네이티브 적용 함수에 도달하지 않는다. 다음 비교는
  `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-category1-selection-20260617`에서 `LOGH_ACTION_LIST_CATEGORY=1`을
  보내, 선택 payload entry가 0이 아닐 때 `list-selection-change`와 `category-apply`가 살아나는지 본다.

### 2026-06-17 - G006 C002: 범주 1 비교 결과와 0x0707 판정 정정
- 범주 1 비교 세션 `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-category1-selection-20260617`에서
  `LOGH_ACTION_LIST_CATEGORY=1`을 보냈다. Trace의 fixed `0x0323`과 compact `0x0356` 모두
  `recordSeatChar254=1`로 들어갔고, Frida 초기 snapshot도 `listCount188=1`,
  `payloadCount270=1`, `firstEntryWord274=1`, `firstEntryDword274=1`이었다.
- 실제 클릭 후 `target-global-rect`는 리스트 row global rect `1081..1397 x 810..842` 안에서
  `resultLowByte=1`, object `stateB02=1`까지 기록했다. 하지만 `listSelected189`는 계속 `-1`이고
  `list-selection-change`, `category-resolve`, `category-apply`, `menu-row-hit`, `factory-dispatch`는 없었다.
  서버 trace도 `0x0300` heartbeat만 보였고 `0x0b01/0x0b07`은 없었다.
- 결론: 현재 blocker는 범주 0의 zero entry만으로 설명되지 않는다. Entry가 `1`이어도 네이티브 UI가
  row hit를 선택 커밋으로 승격하지 않는다. 다음 역추적 대상은 return address `0x00501762` /
  `0x00501dee` 주변의 mouse/button/up/down 처리와 실제 selection setter다.
- `LOGH_ACTION_LIST_APPOINTMENT=1`의 `0x0707`은 서버 trace에는 찍히지만 선부착 Frida 훅에서
  `dispatcher-0707-enter`, `find-unit-*`, `appointment-apply-*`가 전혀 없었다. 따라서 현 단계에서
  `0x0707`은 opt-in wire candidate일 뿐, 네이티브 client-apply 경로로 주장하지 않는다.
- 증거 파일: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-category-retarget-and-0707-rebuttal-20260617.txt`.

### 2026-06-17 - G006 C002: 선택/범주 적용은 통과, 명령 테이블 rowCount가 0
- 정정: 직전 결론의 "selection setter가 아직 미확인"은 최신 final gate 계측으로 좁혀졌다. 범주 0
  세션 `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-category0-final-gate-47900-20260617`에서 `listSelected189 -1->0`,
  `FUN_004f6b00 retval=0`, `FUN_004f5cb0(category=0)` 호출과 반환값 `1`을 확인했다. 따라서 현재
  안정 blocker는 선택 커밋 전이 아니라 `FUN_004f5cb0` 이후 명령 row 생성 단계다.
- 범주 0 결과: 초기 `rowCountD4=24`, `categoryD6=-1`, `firstEntryWord274=0`에서 모드 `1->2`,
  리스트 선택 `-1->0`, category apply 후 `categoryD6=0`이 됐지만 `rowCountD4=0`,
  `selectedCode=null`로 접혔다. 서버 trace는 heartbeat `0x0300`뿐이고 inbound `0x0b01`은 없었다.
- 범주 1 결과: prior safe 세션 `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-final-hit-gate-safe-20260617`은
  `firstEntryWord274=1`, `listSelected189 -1->0`, `FUN_004f6b00 retval=1`까지 갔다. 이후 한 번
  `0xc0000005 offset 0x001034e9`가 있었지만, 재실행
  `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-category1-crash-pointer-47900-20260617`에서는 클라이언트가 살아 있고
  이미 `modeF4=3`, `categoryD6=1`, `rowCountD4=0`인 상태를 보였다. 즉 범주 1도 안정 실패 상태는
  command row 0개다.
- crash 정적 해석: VA `0x005034e9`는 `FUN_005034d0`의 `mov cl,[eax+8]`로, invalid label/widget
  포인터일 때 죽는 위치다. 그러나 범주 0 filtered run의 label write 6회는 모두 유효 포인터
  (`0x718c0a4`..`0x71901b8`)였고 crash가 재현되지 않았다. 이를 현재 blocker로 삼지 않는다.
- 다음 타깃: `FUN_004c8700()` runtime command table. `FUN_004f5cb0`는 per-category record의
  `record+0x14` command count와 `record+0x16` factory list를 읽는다. 현재 범주 0/1에서 이 값이
  0으로 보이므로, table guard/base, category record, 그리고 이를 채우는 parser/dispatcher/store XREF를
  먼저 계측한다. `0x0305/0x0307`, `0x0356`, `0x0707`은 해결책으로 재주장하지 않는다.
- 증거 파일: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-category-apply-rowcount-zero-20260617.txt`.

### 2026-06-17 - G006 C002: command table lifecycle 계측으로 빈 staging 승격 확인
- 세션 `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-command-table-lifecycle-47900-20260617`에서
  `FUN_004ba2b0`, `FUN_004c2a30`, `FUN_004c4a10`, `FUN_004f5cb0`를 한 번에 훅했다. 서버 환경은 범주 0
  final gate와 같은 safe full-world 조합이며 `LOGH_DUTY_CARDS*`, `LOGH_ROSTER_PUSH`,
  `LOGH_STRAT_GRID_EARLY`는 켜지 않았다.
- live `0x0305` dispatcher leave 후 `staging305.count00=0`,
  `staging305.category0.commandCount14=0`이었다. 헤더 바이트는
  `00001cbb0108000000000072006900740073006100726800200049005600...`처럼 문자열성 세션/캐릭터
  바디로 채워졌고, `factories16=[104,32,73,86,0,6,21760,17152]` 같은 값은 보였지만
  count byte가 0이므로 명령 factory 배열로 쓰이지 않는다.
- live `0x0307` dispatcher leave 후에도 `staging307.count00=0`이었다. 이어진
  `FUN_004c2a30 -> FUN_004c4a10`에서 이 staging 상태가 그대로 runtime으로 복사되고,
  `runtime305.guard00=1`, `runtime305.bodyCount08=0`,
  `runtime305.category0.commandCount14=0`, `runtime307.count00=0`이 됐다.
- 범주 적용 직전 `menu.rowCountD4=24`, `selectionAb0=0`, `categoryD6=-1`이었지만
  `FUN_004f5cb0(0)` 직후 `retval=1`, `categoryD6=0`, `rowCountD4=0`으로 접혔다.
  서버 trace에는 heartbeat `0x0300`만 남고 `0x0b01`은 없었다.
- 판정: `FUN_004f5cb0` 실패는 선택/범주/`0x0356` 문제가 아니라 `FUN_004c4a10`이 이미
  commandCount 0인 staging을 guard=1 runtime table로 확정하기 때문이다. 다음 타깃은
  `0x0305/0x0307` 재주입이 아니라 command table을 실제로 nonzero로 만드는 네이티브 경로 또는
  클라 로컬 static resource/dat 파일이다.
- 증거 파일: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-command-table-lifecycle-20260617.txt`,
  raw JSONL `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-command-table-lifecycle-47900-20260617/command_table_lifecycle.jsonl`.

### 2026-06-17 - G006 C002: positive-control과 safe path의 command table 차이 확정
- 과거 positive-control `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-selection-force-nocontent-20260617/table_patch_positive_probe.jsonl`을
  최신 lifecycle 세션과 비교했다. Positive-control은 runtime table에 `tableBase+0x1e=2`,
  `tableBase+0x20=0x002b`, `tableBase+0x22=0x0041`만 쓴 뒤
  `FUN_004f5cb0(commandMenu,0)` 직접 호출로 `result=1`, `afterMenu.categoryD6=0`,
  `afterMenu.rowCountD4=2`, rows `{0x002b,0x0041}`를 만들었다.
- Safe full-world path는 같은 native UI 함수와 같은 category 0 흐름까지 도달하지만, lifecycle 계측에서
  `runtime305.category0.commandCount14=0` 상태로 `FUN_004f5cb0(0)`에 들어가고, 반환 후
  `rowCountD4=0`이 된다. 따라서 native command-row 렌더링 및 `0x002b/0x0041` factory 자체는
  유효하고, 실패 원인은 table source가 nonzero로 seed되지 않는 데 있다.
- 정적 대응: `FUN_004f5cb0`가 읽는 `record+0x14/+0x16`은 positive-control의
  `tableBase+0x1e/+0x20`과 동일 위치다. `FUN_004c4a10`은 staging
  `clientBase+0x3e0c8c/+0x3e5e96`를 runtime `clientBase+0x3416d8/+0x3468ea`로 one-shot
  복사한다. 그러므로 다음 RE는 `FUN_004c4a10` 이전 staging writer/admission/resource 경로를 찾아야 한다.
- 증거 파일: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-command-table-positive-control-compare-20260617.txt`.

### 2026-06-17 - G006 C002: 0x0305/0x0307 wire와 dispatcher body tail 분리
- 목적: 이전 lifecycle 판정에서 `0x0305/0x0307` dispatcher `param_3` head에 보인
  `Friedrich IV`류 문자열이 실제 서버 wire인지, 수신 객체 잔여 메모리인지 분리한다.
- 서버 계측: `src/server/logh7-auth-server.mjs`의 trace field에 generic world-info `0x0305/0x0307`
  요약을 추가했다. raw hex를 남기지 않고 `worldInfoWireLength`, `worldInfoWireCountLe0`,
  `worldInfoWireCountBe0`, `worldInfoWireNonzeroFirst256`, `worldInfoWireAllZeroFirst256`만 기록한다.
  `tests/server/logh7-auth-server.test.mjs`는 이 요약이 raw hex 없이 zero-filled body를 보고하는지 고정한다.
- 실클라 세션: `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-wire-body-residue-47900-20260617`은 safe full-world 환경,
  canonical playable EXE SHA `1f7fad439af2fc7f775b4cdfb2a8e10111ebd5209f98dab8905c9b3b238cc00c`로
  로그인/캐릭터 선택/월드 진입을 재현했다. `LOGH_DUTY_CARDS*`, `LOGH_ROSTER_PUSH`,
  `LOGH_STRAT_GRID_EARLY`는 켜지 않았다.
- wire 결과: 서버 trace에서 `0x0304->0x0305`는 `respLen=21008`, body `21002`B,
  `countLe0=0`, `countBe0=0`, first 256B nonzero 수 `0`이었다. `0x0306->0x0307`도
  `respLen=58808`, body `58802`B, count `0`, first 256B nonzero 수 `0`이었다.
- dispatcher 결과: 같은 순간 Frida `FUN_004ba2b0` 훅은 `param_3` head에
  `000000001cbb0108...0072006900740073006100726800200049005600...` tail을 보았다.
  함수 반환 후 staging은 이 tail 일부를 들고 있었지만 `staging305.count00=0`,
  `staging307.count00=0`, `runtime305.category0.commandCount14=0`이었다.
- 정정: 이전 "live 0x0305/0x0307 body가 Friedrich IV류 세션/캐릭터 데이터" 표현은 너무 강했다.
  현재 증거는 실제 서버 wire가 zero-filled이고, Frida body pointer의 문자열은 이전 lobby/session 수신 버퍼
  잔여 바이트임을 지지한다. 이 tail은 wire 증거가 아니라 "count 0이어도 receive-object buffer tail이
  staging으로 복사될 수 있다"는 증거로만 사용한다.
- 다음 타깃: positive-control과 같은 nonzero `record+0x14/+0x16`이 `FUN_004c4a10` 이전 staging에
  들어가는 원본 resource/dat writer 또는 정확한 nonzero admission shape를 찾는다. `0x0356`, `0x0707`,
  stale `0x0305/0x0307` tail 해석은 반복하지 않는다.
- 증거 파일: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-wire-zero-body-residue-20260617.txt`,
  raw trace `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-wire-body-residue-47900-20260617/trace.jsonl`,
  raw Frida `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-wire-body-residue-47900-20260617/command_table_lifecycle.jsonl`.

### 2026-06-17 - G006 C002: 원본 static command table raw scan 판정
- 대상: `.omo/work/logh7-installed`와 `.omo/work/logh7-extracted`에서 generated runtime/content 트리를 제외한
  MsgDat `.dat/.jpbak`, Face `.tcf/tcf.hed`, `window*.dat`, EXE 후보 96개를 스캔했다.
- 구조 스캔: `0x0305` body shape(`count u16`, 70B stride, `record+0x14` command count,
  `record+0x16` u16 factory list)와 `0x0307` body shape(`count u16`, 196B stride,
  `record+0x02` command count, 8B command descriptors)를 raw offset별로 검사했다.
  후보 27개 파일이 나왔지만 대부분 PE instruction bytes, MsgDat offset/text bytes, 또는 TCF 압축/픽셀성
  raw bytes가 작은 count/command-count predicate를 우연히 만족한 false positive다.
- literal 스캔: positive-control과 가까운 `command_count=2 + {0x002b,0x0041}` 및
  `{0x002b,0x0041}` factory byte열을 별도로 찾았다. 유일한 hit는 installed `G7Start.exe`
  offset `0x28066`의 `...afb541002b00...`였다. 추출 원본 `G7Start.exe` 대응 파일이 없고,
  count/stride-compatible record도 아니며, 런처 표면이므로 게임 클라 staging source 증거로 채택하지 않는다.
- 판정: 원본 MsgDat/static resource raw 파일에서 authoritative command table은 아직 발견되지 않았다.
  같은 raw scan 반복은 가치가 낮다. 다음 타깃은 `FUN_004c4a10` 이전 staging을 nonzero로 만드는
  네이티브 admission/resource decoder, 또는 실제 클라이언트로 검증되는 정확한 nonzero `0x0305/0x0307`
  body shape다.
- 증거 파일: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-original-static-command-table-scan-verdict-20260617.txt`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-original-static-command-table-scan-20260617.json`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-command-factory-literal-scan-20260617.txt`.

### 2026-06-17 - G006 C002: compact 0x0305/0x0307 preload가 runtime command table까지 승격
- 실클라 세션 `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-command-table-preload-probe-v3-47900-20260617`에서
  `LOGH_COMMAND_TABLE_PRELOAD_PROBE=1` 경로를 검증했다. `0x0304`의 정상 empty `0x0305`는 유지하고,
  extra compact nonzero `0x0305`를 전송한 뒤, `0x0306`에는 populated compact `0x0307`을 직접 응답했다.
  이 순서가 이후 empty `0x0307` overwrite를 막았다.
- 서버 trace: 정상 `0x0305`는 `countLe0=0`, `countBe0=0`, first 256B nonzero `0`이었다. extra `0x0305`와
  `0x0307`은 `countLe0=256`, `countBe0=1`, first 256B nonzero `4`로 기록됐다.
- Frida lifecycle: probe `0x0305` 뒤 `staging305.count00=1`,
  `staging305.category0.commandCount14=2`, first factories `0x002b/0x0041`; probe `0x0307` 뒤
  `staging307.count00=1`; `FUN_004c4a10` 뒤 `runtime305.guard00=1`, `runtime305.bodyCount08=1`,
  `runtime305.category0.commandCount14=2`, `runtime307.count00=1`이었다.
- 판정: 반박된 것은 모든 `0x0305/0x0307` 경로가 아니라 잘못된 fixed/static-card body family와 overwrite
  timing이었다. real-client-gated compact body shape는 staging과 runtime command table까지 승격된다.
- 남은 blocker: 같은 세션의 bottom-right command-list click은 time sync만 만들었고, `category-apply` hook,
  inbound `0x0b01`, mined equivalent command는 없었다. 다음 RE는 nonzero runtime command table 상태에서
  실제 menu apply/hit-test/command dispatcher를 추적한다.
- 증거 파일: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-command-table-preload-v3-20260617.md`,
  raw trace `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-command-table-preload-probe-v3-47900-20260617/trace.jsonl`,
  raw Frida `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-command-table-preload-probe-v3-47900-20260617/command_table_lifecycle.jsonl`.

### 2026-06-17 - G006 C002: v5 command-menu activation 반례 정리
- 세션 `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-command-table-menu-activation-v5-47900-20260617`은
  `LOGH_COMMAND_TABLE_PRELOAD_PROBE=1` 상태로 다시 실행했다. lifecycle hook은 v3와 같이
  `staging305.count00=1`, `category0.commandCount14=2`, factory `0x002b/0x0041`,
  `staging307.count00=1`, `runtime305.guard00=1`, `bodyCount08=1`,
  `runtime305.category0.commandCount14=2`, `runtime307.count00=1`을 확인했다.
- `1146,948` 클릭은 우측 패널을 열었고, `1146,985` 클릭은 화면상 `1. 국가관리` 행을 맞혔다.
  all-hit stdout은 해당 hit를 `object=0x7157f10`, `idB04=11`, `x=1084`, `y=97`, `w=160`, `h=16`,
  `returnVa=0x501dee`로 기록했다. 이것은 command-menu row가 아니라 system/info-panel 행이다.
- `modeButton24/28` 후보도 우측 상단 `게임 중단`/`사운드 설정` rect로 정정한다.
  각각 `1073..1238/875..907`, `1244..1401/875..907`이며, `662,924` 클릭은 전략 mode/category
  전환을 만들지 않았다.
- category/menu hook의 마지막 상태는 `dispatch0356=1`, `tray0356=1`, `listApply=3`,
  `listScanChange=2`, `categoryResolve=0`, `categoryApply=0`, `rowHit=0`,
  `listSelected189=-1`, `menuRowCountD4=24`, `menuCategoryD6=-1`이다.
- trace의 `0x0bxx`는 서버 선푸시 `0x0b09/0x0b0a`뿐이고 inbound `0x0b01`/`0x0b07`은 없다.
  종료는 `socket-error read ECONNRESET`.
- `direct_category_apply_probe.js`는 문법 검사를 통과했지만 client PID `39180` 종료 뒤 attach되어
  `frida.ProcessNotFoundError`만 남겼다. 다음 반복은 월드 진입 직후 direct category apply를 먼저 붙인다.
- 증거 파일: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-command-menu-activation-v5-20260617.md`.

  `FUN_004f5cb0(0)` again kept `rowCountD4=2`, but `FUN_005015f0(kind=2)` still recorded 35 hit-route

- Refutes/Confirms: confirms command-table admission, category apply, and row object creation all work in this
  controlled path; refutes treating direct apply or mode/selection scalar forcing as sufficient for playability.
  G006 C002 remains pending because command rows are not attached to the active `0x005025f0` /

### 2026-06-17 - G006 C002: v8 commandMenu active gate controls row loop admission
- Scope: continued from v7. The target was not another command table admission test; it was the exact reason
  `FUN_004f58c0` did not pass command rows to `FUN_005015f0(kind=2)`.
- Session: `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-row-attach-v8-47900-20260617`, real client PID `33804`.
  The session stopped with canonical playable SHA
  `1f7fad439af2fc7f775b4cdfb2a8e10111ebd5209f98dab8905c9b3b238cc00c` restored; port 47900 was closed afterward.
- Direct apply still works: `row_attach_probe.jsonl` records `FUN_004f5cb0(commandMenu,0)` success,
  `rowCountD4=2`, `categoryD6=0`, row0 `0x137388e4/idB04=23`, row1 `0x137397fc/idB04=650`.
- Reference scan: after apply, durable row refs were only `commandMenu+0x30/+0x34` and equivalent
  `hud+0x160/+0x164`. Process-wide refs were transient stack/scratch hits, not evidence of a durable active widget
  tree.
- Gate finding: static `FUN_004f58c0` requires `*(commandMenu[0]+4) != 0` before it loops row objects. Live
  `row_scan_gate_dump.jsonl` showed `commandMenu.activePtr=0x0fba0e40`, `activePtr+4=0`,
  `rowListCount620=0`, `rowBuffer628=null` after direct apply.
- Diagnostic positive control: `enable_command_menu_gate_probe.jsonl` wrote `activePtr+4` from `0` to `1`.
  `post_gate_row_hit_probe.jsonl` then recorded row0 and row1 reaching `FUN_005015f0(kind=2)`, both with
  `hit=false`. Re-clicking `1146,985` in `post_gate_row_hit_click_probe.jsonl` kept the same false hits and server
  trace remained `0x0f08->0x0f09` plus heartbeats, with no `0x0b01`/`0x0b07`.
- Refutes/Confirms: confirms v7's route absence is due first to `commandMenu[0]+4 == 0`; forcing that byte is enough
  to admit rows into the row-loop hit-test path. Refutes claiming this completes C002 because row hit remains false
  and no command packet is emitted.
- Next target: find the native writer that should set `commandMenu[0]+4`, likely through mode/widget enablement
  around `FUN_004fd7a0` or related object activation, then trace `FUN_005025f0` / coordinate transform until command
  row hit returns true.
- Evidence files: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-row-active-gate-v8-20260617.md`,
