  `FUN_00581c80` SelectGrid factory, `FUN_0058fef0` command gate, and `FUN_005737d0` SendWarpCommand remained
  zero.
- Verdict: G006 C002 remains pending. v9 moves the blocker past row admission/coordinate hit and into the boundary
  after `FUN_004f93c0(0x2b)`: dump the runtime factory table slot and returned object to determine why row0 does not
  construct SelectGrid. Evidence: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-gate-pair-v9-20260617.md`,
  `gate_pair_probe_fixed2.jsonl`, `row_center_click_probe_filtered2.jsonl`, and `selectgrid_target_probe.jsonl`.

### 2026-06-17 - G006 C002: v10 factory-return result corrects v9 SelectGrid boundary
- Session: `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-factory-return-v10-47900-20260617`, real client PID `49012`,
  server PID `31320`, canonical playable SHA
  `1f7fad439af2fc7f775b4cdfb2a8e10111ebd5209f98dab8905c9b3b238cc00c`.
- Probe: `factory_return_probe_v10b.js` hooked `0x004f93c0`, `0x00581c80`, `0x0058fef0`,
  `0x005737d0`, and `0x004b78a0` before row0 click. The broader `factory_return_probe_v10.js` was
  superseded because it flooded receive/result events.
- Runtime slot result: `factoryTable=0xc9e2e0`, `slot2bAddress=0xc9e3a8`, `slot2b=0x581c80`, and
  `selectGridFactory=0x581c80`. Thus slot `0x2b` is actually `FUN_00581c80` in the live client.
- Row0 result: row0 center `(57,146)` entered `FUN_004f93c0(index=43/0x2b, category=0)` with
  `selectedD5=0`; `FUN_00581c80` entered once with `arg1=0x113108e4`, `arg2=0xc9e768`, returned
  object `0x544db60` vtable `0x6702b8`; dispatcher returned `1`, manager count changed `2->3`, current
  dialog became `0x544db60`, and returned object `+0x28` became `0x2b`.
- Correction: v9's "SelectGrid 0 calls" was an observer timing problem after row click. The blocker is no
  longer factory-slot or SelectGrid construction. It is after SelectGrid is linked.
- Target/confirm result: target click `(833,545)` displayed a selected target and `90 LY`, but Frida only
  recorded `FUN_004b78a0(arg1=1,arg2=0x45,arg3=0x19fbd8,arg4=0x02199b4c)` returning `0`. Static
  `FUN_004b78a0` maps `arg2=0x45` to switch case `0x44`, request/response `0x0f08/0x0f09`.
  Re-clicking `워프 항행`, pressing `RETURN`, and repeating the target click did not call `FUN_0058fef0`
  or `FUN_005737d0`.
- Trace discriminator: final trace has `0x0f08` twice and `0x0f09` twice, plus heartbeats, but no inbound
  `0x0b01` and no outbound `0x0b07`.

### 2026-06-18 - G006 C002: v28 current-grid raw routing correction
- Outcome: C002 remains pending. v28 narrows H1/H2 but does not identify a proven `DAT_007cd04c+0x11178` writer.
- Static client facts:
  - `0x00011178` immediate appears in six code references only: `0x004d4e9c`, `0x004d5116`, `0x004d6392`,
    `0x004d6494`, `0x004d6f79`, `0x004d8f41`. All are reads from `DAT_007cd04c+0x11178`.
  - Direct global-store patterns to `DAT_007cd04c` using `a3`, `c7 05`, `89 0d`, and `89 15` were not found.
  - `FUN_004d3a40` is the strongest writer/initializer for the structure behind `DAT_007cd04c`: it starts at
    `DAT_007cd04c+8`, loops 100 cells per row, and advances the destination by `0x0e` bytes per cell. This confirms
    the expanded 100x50 grid layout but not the `+0x11178` writer.
  - `FUN_0057bbc0` reads count/list at `+0x1117c/+0x11180` with `0x60` stride; current evidence shows it as a
    consumer, not an initializer.
- Server/wire facts:
  - `0x0317 ResponseInformationGrid` is the only implemented current-grid dword record, but `FUN_004ba2b0` case
    `0x0317` writes it to `clientBase+0x35f358`. This is separate from `DAT_007cd04c+0x11178`.
  - `0x0313/0x0315` fill the clientBase strategic grid/object tables consumed by `FUN_004c8b70`, not the
    `DAT_007cd04c` expanded structure directly.

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v30 global slot writer watch
- Goal: identify who initializes or writes the BSS/global slot `DAT_007cd04c` and neighboring guard slot
  `DAT_007cd048`, after v29 refuted separated server-delivery variants.
- References read this round: `omo:ulw-loop/references/full-workflow.md`, `omo:debugging/references/runtimes/native-binary.md`,
  `omo:debugging/references/tools/ghidra.md`, `omo:debugging/references/methodology/00-setup.md`,
  `omo:debugging/references/methodology/02-investigate.md`, and the official Frida JavaScript API for
  `MemoryAccessMonitor`.
- Hypotheses:
  1. [OPEN] `DAT_007cd04c` is assigned by an indirect/common initializer rather than any direct immediate store.
     Distinguishing evidence: slot-page access monitor or function hooks show the slot going null -> non-null and a
     `details.from` / hook frame near a setup function.
  2. [OPEN] `MemoryAccessMonitor` may only report the first page access after each arm, so read-heavy code can hide the
     write. Distinguishing evidence: only read accesses are captured while periodic snapshots still show slot changes.
  3. [OPEN] `DAT_007cd04c` may be initialized before the attach point even with `start --no-login`.
     Distinguishing evidence: first `watch-ready` snapshot already has a non-null `DAT_007cd04c`.

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v31 heap allocation discriminator
- Goal: find the allocator that returns the eventual `DAT_007cd04c` root pointer, after v30c proved the slot changes
  between the `0x0f02` world-init response bundle and the later `0x0f06` request.
- Hypotheses:
  1. [OPEN] The root block is allocated by the client new-like wrapper `FUN_00648d42` or CRT `_malloc`.
     Distinguishing evidence: an allocation record returns the same pointer later seen in `DAT_007cd04c`.
  2. [OPEN] The root block is allocated by `HeapAlloc` through `FUN_005ffaf5` / `FUN_005ffc34` wrappers.
     Distinguishing evidence: wrapper/OS hook returns the eventual root pointer or a near pointer with size around
     `0x11178..0x20000`.
  3. [OPEN] The pointer is not a fresh heap allocation during this window; it is taken from an object pool or member
     field populated earlier. Distinguishing evidence: slot poll changes to a pointer with no matching allocation record
     in the window, while allocator hooks are installed and report other allocations.
- Planned artifacts:
  - [ ] `tools/logh7_heap_slot_watch.py` - Frida allocator hook and `DAT_007cd04c` slot poll tool.
  - [ ] `tools/tests/test_logh7_heap_slot_watch.py` - focused CLI/JS coverage.
  - [ ] `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-heap-slot-v31-47900-20260618/` - bounded real-client safe-env session.
  - [ ] `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-heap-slot-watch-v31-20260618.jsonl` - allocator/slot watch output.
  - [ ] `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-heap-slot-watch-v31-start.json` - UI explorer start transcript.
  - [ ] `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-heap-slot-watch-v31-login.json` - login transcript.
  - [ ] `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-heap-slot-watch-v31-game-start.json` - game-start click transcript.

  allocator size filter from `0x10000..0x20000` to `0x1000..0x200000` while attaching only after character select.
- Additional planned artifacts for wide allocation retry:
  - [ ] `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-heap-slot-v31c-47900-20260618/` - safe-env session advanced to character select
    before allocator attach.
  - [ ] `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-heap-slot-watch-v31c-wide-20260618.jsonl` - wide allocator/slot watch output.
  - [ ] `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-heap-slot-watch-v31c-wide-summary.json` - parsed wide allocation summary.
  - [ ] `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-heap-slot-watch-v31c-cleanup.txt` - cleanup receipt.
- Final v30/v31 synthesis:
  - v30c stage2 reached `0x0f07` and proved `DAT_007cd04c` flips from null to `0xf5e7918` at
    `2026-06-18T01:42:12.139Z`, after `0x0f02` extras at `01:42:11.584Z..01:42:11.587Z` and before `0x0f06` at
    `01:42:12.372Z`. `DAT_007cd048` becomes `1` at `01:42:12.327Z`; `FUN_004d3a40` enters at `01:42:12.352Z`,
    after root/guard initialization. `MemoryAccessMonitor` captured only one page read from `0x4e971a` and zero writes.
  - v31b stage2 reached `0x0f07` and proved the same timing class: root `0xf5f0918` appears at
    `2026-06-18T01:51:44.227Z`, after `0x0f02` extras at `01:51:42.026Z..01:51:42.029Z` and before `0x0f06` at
    `01:51:44.902Z`. Hooked allocation wrappers recorded 178 events, but `rootExactAllocationMatches=[]` and
    `nearRootAllocations=[]`.
  - v31c wide allocation retry did not reach `0x0f07` (`matched=false`, `seen=19`) and is an incomplete scenario.
    Cleanup restored canonical playable SHA with `shaVerified=true`; no game/frida/python watcher process or
    `4787/47900/47901` listener remained.
  - Verification: `python -m unittest tools.tests.test_logh7_global_slot_watch tools.tests.test_logh7_heap_slot_watch
    tools.tests.test_logh7_current_grid_watch` -> 6 tests OK; `python -m py_compile` on the two watcher modules and tests
    passed; installed `ruff` passed on the same files.
  - Evidence: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-global-heap-slot-v30-v31-20260618.md`,
    `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-global-heap-slot-timeline-v30-v31-20260618.json`,
    `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-global-slot-watch-v30c-stage2-summary.json`,
    `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-heap-slot-watch-v31b-summary.json`,
    `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-heap-slot-watch-v31c-cleanup.txt`.
  - Next discriminator: find the computed writer between `0x0f02` and `0x0f06`, likely through global-page
    memcpy/memmove/memset overlap filtering or handler-boundary binary search. Do not repeat server payload variants as
    completion evidence.

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v32-v33 global page writer 판별
- 목표: v30/v31에서 좁힌 `0x0f02` 뒤, `0x0f06` 전 window 안에서 `DAT_007cd04c` 루트 슬롯을 실제로
  쓰는 computed writer를 찾는다.
- 추가 도구:
  - `tools/logh7_global_page_write_watch.py`: `0x007cd040..0x007cd060`과 겹치는
    `memcpy`/`memmove`/`memset`/Rtl/lstr/internal `_memset` 호출을 기록한다.
  - `tools/logh7_global_page_guard_watch.py`: Frida `Process.setExceptionHandler`와 `Memory.protect`로
    `0x007cd000` page를 read-only로 바꿔 write fault를 잡고, fault 뒤 page를 다시 arm한다.
- v32 결과: safe env에서 `0x0f07`까지 도달했고 `DAT_007cd04c=0xf5e7918`, `DAT_007cd048=1` 변화를
  봤지만, 18개 copy/fill hook에서 `overlap-write`는 0개였다. 루트 writer는 이 표면이 아니었다.
- v33 결과: safe env에서 `0x0f07`까지 도달했고 page-guard가 26개 write fault를 기록했다. 감시 범위
  target hit는 2개였고, 루트 슬롯 write는 `2026-06-18T02:11:15.593Z`의
  `EIP=0x004c8a23`, `memory=0x007cd04c`였다. 바로 다음 poll에서 `DAT_007cd04c=0xf5f1918`이
  보였다.
- 정적 매핑: `0x004c8a23`은 `FUN_004c8a10` 내부의
  `*(undefined4 *)(param_1 + 4) = param_2` 대입이다. fault 시점의 `param_1`은 `0x007cd048`
  전역 상태 객체이므로 이 명령이 `DAT_007cd04c` 루트 포인터 writer다.
- 후속 target hit `0x004c8bd0 -> 0x007cd050`은 `FUN_004c8bc0` 인접 field/table 초기화로 매핑된다.
  이것은 루트 대입 뒤 실행되는 경로이며 root writer가 아니다.
- 아직 미완료: root assignment 뒤에도 `currentRaw11178=0`, `listCount1117c=0`이다. 따라서 C002는
  pending이다. 다음 판별은 `FUN_004c8a10` entry args, `param_2` 출처, `FUN_004d3bd0` /
  `FUN_004c8bc0` / `FUN_004d3a40` 전후 root field snapshot을 잡아 `+0x11178/+0x1117c/+0x11180`
  writer를 찾는 것이다.
- 검증/정리: v33 cleanup은 canonical playable SHA `shaVerified=true`, 게임/Frida/Python watcher
  프로세스 없음, `4787/47900/47901` listener 없음이었다.
- 증거: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-pageguard-v32-v33-20260618.md`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-pagewrite-v32-20260618.jsonl`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-pageguard-v33-20260618.jsonl`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-pageguard-v33-stop.json`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-pageguard-v33-cleanup.txt`.

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v34 root initializer boundary 판별
- 목표: v33에서 찾은 `FUN_004c8a10` root 대입 전후로 `DAT_007cd04c+0x11178/+0x1117c/+0x11180`
  writer가 실행되는지 확인한다.
- 추가 도구: `tools/logh7_root_init_watch.py`와 `tools/tests/test_logh7_root_init_watch.py`. 도구는
  `FUN_004c8a10`, `FUN_004d3bd0`, `FUN_004c8bc0`, `FUN_004d3a40`, `FUN_004b64c0`,
  `FUN_004c4170` entry/leave에서 root fields, caller args, `DAT_007c1b4c+0x2a418` snapshot을 남긴다.
- 검증: red-first test는 모듈 부재로 실패했고, 구현 뒤 root-init 단독 2 tests OK, watcher 묶음 12 tests OK,
  `py_compile` OK, installed Ruff OK. `tools/logh7_root_init_watch.py` pure LOC는 182다.
- v34 실클라 결과: safe env에서 `0x0f07`이 `2026-06-18T02:19:43.098Z`에 도달했고 watcher event 22개를
  기록했다.
- 핵심 관측:
  - `FUN_004c8a10` entry: `ecx=0x007cd048`, `rootParam2=0xf5ef918`, `stackArg2=0xf34a020`.
    이때 `rootParam2Fields`는 이미 `byte0=1`, `currentRaw11178=0`, `listCount1117c=0`, grid head zero였다.
  - `FUN_004d3bd0` entry/leave: global root는 `0xf5ef918`이지만 current/list/grid head는 계속 0/zero였다.
    manager snapshot은 `DAT_007c1b4c=0x9060048`, `field2a418_ptr=0xe249fd0`이었다.
  - `FUN_004c8bc0` entry/leave: current/list/grid head는 계속 0/zero였다.
  - `FUN_004c8a10` leave: guard는 1이 됐지만 `currentRaw11178=0`, `listCount1117c=0`이었다.
  - `FUN_004d3a40` entry/leave: guard 1 상태에서도 current/list/grid head는 계속 0/zero였다.
- 판정: `FUN_004c8a10`은 root pointer를 연결할 뿐 root object 본문을 채우지 않는다.
  `FUN_004d3bd0`, `FUN_004c8bc0`, `FUN_004d3a40`도 v34 경로에서는 `+0x11178/+0x1117c/+0x11180`
  writer가 아니다. 다음 blocker는 `rootParam2` 객체가 `FUN_004c8a10`에 들어오기 전 어디서 생성되고
  채워져야 하는지다.
- 다음 판별: `FUN_004c4170` 내부 `FUN_004b5bb0 -> FUN_004c45f0(uVar2,2)` 경계를 hook하고,
  `FUN_004b64c0` entry의 `edx` root candidate를 잡은 즉시 root object page/range guard를 건다.
- 정리: v34 cleanup은 canonical playable SHA `shaVerified=true`, 게임/Frida/Python watcher 프로세스 없음,
  `4787/47900/47901` listener 없음이었다. `47900` TIME_WAIT만 남았다.
- 증거: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-root-init-v34-20260618.md`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-root-init-v34-20260618.jsonl`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-root-init-v34-wait-0f07.json`,

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v35/v36b root source 판별
- 목표: v34가 남긴 `FUN_004c4170` pre-assignment boundary에서 base/institution source가 비어 있어 root list가
  비는지, 아니면 current/focus 필드가 별도 blocker인지 판별한다.
- 서버 구현: `LOGH_WORLD_IMPORT_BASES=1` opt-in을 추가했다. `LOGH_WORLD_PLAYER=1` 상태에서 `0x0f02`
  world-grid initialize를 처리할 때 `0x0f03` ack 전에 `0x031f ResponseInformationBase`와
  `0x0321 ResponseInformationInstitution`을 extra inner로 보낸다. 기본 safe path에는 영향이 없다.
- 테스트:
  - Red-first: `tests/server/logh7-login-session.test.mjs`의 신규 테스트가 기존 코드에서
    observed codes `[0x0325, 0x0323, 0x0f03]`로 실패했다. 기대는
    `[0x031f, 0x0321, 0x0325, 0x0323, 0x0f03]`였다.
  - Green: focused test 통과 후 `node --test tests/server/logh7-login-session.test.mjs`가 82 tests OK.
- v35 baseline:
  - safe env에서 `0x0f02` 후 `0x0204`, `0x0313`, `0x0315`, `0x0325`, `0x0323`, `0x033b`, `0x0f03` 순서였다.
    `0x031f`/`0x0321`은 없었다.
  - `0x0f06->0x0f07`은 `2026-06-18T02:25:56.337Z..02:25:56.338Z`에 도달했다.
  - watcher는 `FUN_004c4170` enter/leave에서 base/institution source와 copied buffers가 zero임을 보였고,
    `FUN_004c8a10` entry의 `rootParam2Fields`도 `byte0=1`, `currentRaw11178=0`, `listCount1117c=0`이었다.
- v36b opt-in:
  - 첫 v36은 `LOGH_WORLD_IMPORT_BASES=1`만 넣고 known-safe flags를 누락해 폐기했다. cleanup SHA만 확인했고
    completion evidence로 쓰지 않는다.
  - corrected v36b는 `0x0f02` 후 `0x0204`, `0x031f`, `0x0321`, `0x0313`, `0x0315`, `0x0325`,
    `0x0323`, `0x033b`, `0x0f03` 순서였다. `0x031f`은 `respLen=1546`, `0x0321`은
    `respLen=36330`이었다.
  - `0x0f06->0x0f07`은 `2026-06-18T02:34:33.228Z..02:34:33.229Z`에 도달했다.
  - watcher는 `FUN_004c4170` enter에서 base/institution source buffers가 nonzero이고, leave에서 copied buffers도
    nonzero로 바뀌었음을 보였다. `FUN_004c8a10` entry/leave의 root fields는 `byte0=1`,
    `currentRaw11178=0`, `listCount1117c=4`였다.
- 정적 해석:
  - `FUN_004b5bb0(param_1)`은 `*(param_1 + 800)`을 반환한다.
  - `FUN_004c45f0(param_1, param_2, param_3)`은 `param_3==2`에서 `param_1+0x2a58f8` 영역을 초기화하고,
    mode field와 `param_1+0x126714 = param_2`를 쓴다.
  - `FUN_004c4170`은 `FUN_004b5bb0`, `FUN_004c45f0(uVar2,2)` 뒤 mode byte 2이면
    `param_1+0x2b6a6c=1`을 세운다. 이후 `param_1+0x3facf4 -> param_1+0x2b6a74`,
    `param_1+0x3fb2f8 -> param_1+0x2b7078`을 복사하고, `param_1+0x2b6a70 = *(param_1+0x126714)`을 쓴다.
- 판정: v36b는 base/institution list source와 list copy path를 통과시켰지만 C002를 닫지 않는다.
  남은 blocker는 `mainState+0x126714`, `mainState+0x2b6a70`, `DAT_007cd04c+0x11178` current/focus source다.
- 다음 판별: `FUN_004c45f0`의 `param_2` 출처와 `mainState+0x126714` writer를 정적/런타임 양쪽에서 찾는다.
  `0x031f/0x0321` preload는 completion evidence로 반복하지 않는다.
- 정리: v36b cleanup은 canonical playable SHA
  `1f7fad439af2fc7f775b4cdfb2a8e10111ebd5209f98dab8905c9b3b238cc00c`를 확인했고, 관련 game/Frida/Python
  watcher process 및 `47900` listener가 남지 않았다.
- 증거: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-root-source-v35-v36b-20260618.md`,

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v37 current-source writer boundary 판별

  - strategy path의 `FUN_004c4170`은 `[mainState+8]`을 `FUN_004b5bb0`에 넘긴다.

    후속 copy에서 `mainState+0x2b6a70`과 `DAT_007cd04c+0x11178`도 zero로 남는다.

  `mainState+8` source object의 `+0x320` writer/parser로 좁혔다. `0x031f/0x0321` preload나
  더 많은 서버 push를 completion evidence로 반복하지 않는다.

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v38 CreateOutfit text-parser 부정 판별

- 목적: v37에서 `FUN_0048fb80` binary parser가 `[mainState+8]+0x320`을 채우지 않는다는
  부정 증거가 나왔으므로, 인접 `FUN_0048ffd0` text/INF-style parser와 그 함수 범위의
  `+0x320` write site도 같은 경계에서 배제한다.
- canonical playable EXE SHA:
  `1f7fad439af2fc7f775b4cdfb2a8e10111ebd5209f98dab8905c9b3b238cc00c`.
- static `+0x320` direct refs:
  `0x0040a816`, `0x0048dea8`, `0x0048e3eb`, `0x0048ff92`, `0x0049086b`,
  `0x00490dcb`, `0x004a4cc8`.
  Vtable/data ref는 `0x0048fb80` at `0x0066d5b4`, `0x0048ffd0` at
  `0x0066d5b8`, `0x0048d860` at `0x0066d614`다.
- 구현: `tools/logh7_root_init_watch.py`에
  `installHook('0x0048ffd0', 'commandCreateOutfitTextParser-0048ffd0');`를 추가했다.
  실패 우선 test는 generated JS에 `0x0048ffd0`과 label이 없어 실패했고, 구현 후
  `python -m unittest tools.tests.test_logh7_root_init_watch`는 2 tests OK였다. watcher 관련
  unittest 12개, `py_compile`, standalone `ruff check`도 통과했다.
- v38 실클라 실행:
  - 세션 `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-root-current-v38-47900-20260618`.
  - 안전 플래그와 `LOGH_WORLD_IMPORT_BASES=1` 사용. 금지 플래그
    `LOGH_NPC_AI`, `LOGH_RELAY`, `LOGH_AUTHORITATIVE`, `LOGH_DUTY_CARDS`,
    `LOGH_ROSTER_PUSH`, `LOGH_STRAT_GRID_EARLY`는 없었다.
  - trace는 로비, 캐릭터 선택, gameplay connection, `0x0f06->0x0f07`, post-load
    `0x0b09/0x0325/0x0323/0x0b0a/0x0356/0x1200/0x1202/0x1201`까지 도달.
- 핵심 watcher 결과:

  - `commandCreateOutfitTextParser-0048ffd0-enter/leave`: 0회.

  후보로 채워지지 않는다. 다음 실행은 서버 payload 변형이 아니라 source object 네이티브 생성,

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v41 source import `+0x320` 판별

- 목표: v40에서 남은 inline `\x01name` source `+0x320` writer를 정적/런타임으로 좁힌다.
- 정적 판정:
  - `0x004b5bd0`: `mov al,[esp+4]; mov [ecx+0x31e],al; ret 4`. `+0x31e` setter다.
  - `0x004b5be0`: `mov eax,[esp+4]; mov [ecx+0x358],eax; ret 4`. `+0x358` setter다.
  - `0x004c2a80`: `0x004b780e`에서 호출되는 source import wrapper다.
  - `0x004c2c80`: source import/copy body다. `0x00771074` `"name"`과 `0x0077107c` `"other"`를
    참조하고 helper `0x005fe270`으로 inline `\x01name` source를 구성한다.
  - optional record path에서 `0x004c2f01 lea edi,[eax+0x318]`,
    `0x004c2f07 mov ecx,0x16`, `0x004c2f0c mov esi,ebx`, `0x004c2f0e rep movsd`가
    source `+0x318` 블록을 채운다. 따라서 source `+0x320`은 optional record `+0x08`에서 온다.
  - 이어 `0x004c2f18 call 0x004b5bd0`은 같은 source의 `+0x31e` byte setter이고,
    `0x004c2f1d` 이후 `0x004b5be0`은 `+0x358` setter다.
- watcher:
  - 새 파일 `tools/logh7_source_import_watch.py`와 test
    `tools/tests/test_logh7_source_import_watch.py`를 추가했다.
  - 최초 red test는 module 부재로 실패했고, 구현 후 focused unittest/`py_compile`/Ruff가 통과했다.
  - v41 실행 뒤 wrapper/copy stack shape가 다름을 반영해 `wrapperFields`와 `importFields`를 분리했다.
- v41 실클라:
  - 세션 `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-source-import-v41-47900-20260618`.
  - canonical playable SHA `1f7fad439af2fc7f775b4cdfb2a8e10111ebd5209f98dab8905c9b3b238cc00c`.
  - safe flags와 `LOGH_WORLD_IMPORT_BASES=1` 사용. 금지 플래그
    `LOGH_NPC_AI`, `LOGH_RELAY`, `LOGH_AUTHORITATIVE`, `LOGH_DUTY_CARDS`,
    `LOGH_ROSTER_PUSH`, `LOGH_STRAT_GRID_EARLY`는 absent.
  - trace는 로비, 캐릭터 선택, gameplay connection, `0x0f06->0x0f07`,
    post-load `0x0b09/0x0325/0x0323/0x0b0a/0x0356/0x1200/0x1202/0x1201`까지 도달했다.
- 핵심 런타임 판정:
  - `sourceImportCallsite-004b780e-hit`: `ecx=0xf349020`,
    `predictedSource=0xf34902c`, `mainSlot8Before=0xf34902c`. 즉
    `[mainState+8]=mainState+0xc` store는 `0x004b780e` 이전에 이미 완료된다.
  - `sourceImportCopy-004c2c80-enter`: `primaryRecord=0xf6b38d4`,
    `optionalRecord=0xf7633e0`, `mainSlot8Before=0xf34902c`, `predictedSource=0xf34902c`.
  - `sourceOptionalCopyAfter-004c2f18-hit`: `ecxSource=0xf34902c`,
    `ebxOptionalRecord=0xf7633e0`, `sourceHeadHex=016e616d65...`,
    `predictedSource320=0`, `optionalRecordPlus08=0`, `source320MatchesOptional08=true`.
- 판정: C002는 pending. `+0x320` writer 자체는 optional record copy 경계로 좁혔지만,
  현재 서버/레코드 데이터의 optional record `+0x08`이 0이라 current/focus가 열리지 않는다.
  다음은 optional record 생성/채움 경로, optional record `+0x08`의 원본 nonzero 기대값,
  `[mainState+8]=mainState+0xc` slot writer를 추적한다.
- 정리: session stopped, 관련 game/Frida/Python watcher process 없음,
  `4787/47900/47901` TCP entry 없음, trace copy SHA 일치. watcher는 17개 이벤트 후
  자동 종료하지 않아 watcher Python PID와 wrapper PowerShell PID를 수동 종료했다.
- 증거: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-source-import-v41-20260618.md`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-source-import-v41-20260618.jsonl`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-source-import-v41-trace.jsonl`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-source-import-v41-cleanup.txt`,
  `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-source-import-v41-47900-20260618/shots/005-v41-character-row1.png`,

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v42-v45 `0x0325` parser-stream split

- 목표: v41에서 좁힌 optional record가 어떤 unit table parser 결과와 연결되는지 확인하고,
  early/postload `0x0325` wire layout을 분리한다.
- 정적 판정:
  - `FUN_00419ca0`은 count를 native output `+0`에 읽은 뒤 `add edi, 8`을 수행하고,
    다음 unit id를 `[edi-4]`, 즉 native output `+4`에 쓴다.
  - 따라서 native memory layout은 `[count u16][pad][unit0 @ +4]`이지만, parser가 읽는
    wire stream에는 count 다음 unit id가 바로 이어진다.
  - `0x004bb15c`는 unit table count가 1이면 `push unit0; push 0; push 1; call 0x004c2c80`로
    exact-count branch를 타며 return은 `0x004bb179`이다.
- 구현:
  - `tools/logh7_source_import_watch.py`에 `characterRecordParser-004301d0`,
    `unitTableParser-00419ca0`, `primaryUnit24`, unit table count/id snapshots를 추가했다.
  - `src/server/logh7-login-protocol.mjs`에 `wireLayout: "parser-stream"` option을 추가했다.
  - `src/server/logh7-login-session.mjs`에는 global `LOGH_UNIT_STREAM_WIRE`와 postload-only
    `LOGH_POSTLOAD_UNIT_STREAM_WIRE` 선택을 분리했다.
  - `src/server/logh7-auth-server.mjs` trace fields는 `unit0IdBe2/unit0IdLe2`를 추가했다.
- RED/GREEN:
  - protocol test는 parser-stream wire가 native count padding 없이 body[2]에 unit id를 쓰는지
    확인한다.
  - session test는 global parser-stream과 postload-only parser-stream replay를 각각 고정한다.
  - `node --test tests/server/logh7-login-protocol.test.mjs tests/server/logh7-login-session.test.mjs`
    132 tests pass.
- v42 baseline:
  - early native `0x0325`는 parser에서 count=256, unit0 id=256, unit1 id=0으로 읽혔다.
  - early source import는 primary id=1이지만 `primaryUnit24=0`, optionalRecord index 1/id0이었다.
  - postload character record에는 `primaryUnit24=1`이 있었지만 early source는 복구하지 못했다.
- v43/v44 반증:
  - global `LOGH_UNIT_STREAM_WIRE=1`은 early unit parser를 count=1/unit0=1로 맞췄다.
  - 그러나 exact-count branch `0x004bb15c -> 0x004bb179`로 들어간 뒤 클라이언트가
    ECONNRESET/창 종료로 끝났다.
  - `LOGH_FULL_UNIT_LOCATION`을 제거한 v44도 같은 crash path였으므로 early parser-stream은
    금지한다.
- v45 안정 판정:
  - `LOGH_POSTLOAD_UNIT_STREAM_WIRE=1`만 켜고 global parser-stream/full-unit-location은 끈다.
  - early `0x0325`는 native-safe count=256/unit0=256 path로 남아 클라이언트가 전략 HUD까지
    살아남았다.
  - postload `0x0325`는 parser-stream으로 replay되어 count=1/unit0=1이 됐다.
  - postload `FUN_004c2c80` 경계는 primary id=1/`primaryUnit24=1`, optional unit0 id=1,
    optionalUnitIndex=0으로 맞았다.
  - `optionalRecord+8=0`이라 `source+0x320`은 계속 0이다.
- UI/상호작용:
  - v45 HUD screenshot에는 하단 좌측 `이미 탈퇴하셨습니다.`가 표시되어 UI message mapping이
    아직 문맥과 맞지 않는다.
  - `(728,552)` click은 `0x0300` time request만 만들었고, `(690,800)`, `(700,985)`는
    유의미한 command를 만들지 않았다. `0x0b01/0x0b07`은 없다.
- 판정: C002는 pending. Early `0x0325` parser-stream 반복은 crash 경로이므로 금지하고,
  postload-only parser-stream은 유지한다. 다음은 실제 clickable object/camera/grid cell path,
  UI message source, optionalRecord `+0x08` writer를 추적한다.
- 정리: v45 session stopped. 추가 점검에서 `G7MTClient.exe`/Frida/Python process와
  `4787/47900/47901` TCP entry가 없었다.
- 증거: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-source-import-v45-postload-stream-minunit-20260618.md`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-source-import-v45-postload-stream-minunit-20260618.jsonl`,
  `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-source-import-v45-postload-stream-minunit-47900-20260618/trace.jsonl`,
  `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-source-import-v45-postload-stream-minunit-47900-20260618/shots/003-v45-character-row1.png`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-source-import-v45-cleanup-20260618.txt`.

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v52 SelectGrid validator X upstream 추적

- 목표: v51에서 보이는 `발할라`/`니플헤임` 클릭이 projection writer와 validator까지 도달하지만
  `FUN_004d6310` x 인자가 `0x007b360c` 같은 pointer-like 값으로 깨지는 원인을 찾는다.
- References read: `ulw-loop/references/full-workflow.md`,
  `debugging/references/runtimes/native-binary.md`,
  `debugging/references/methodology/00-setup.md`,
  `debugging/references/methodology/02-investigate.md`,
  `debugging/references/methodology/08-qa.md`,
  `debugging/references/methodology/09-cleanup.md`.
- 환경 snapshot:
  - Repo HEAD: `813dd282c69c96e15e1aaf165ac60430b32c5969`.
  - Active Codex goal objective matches `.omo/ulw-loop/goals.json` aggregate objective.
  - `omo ulw-loop status --json` under current Codex session id looked for
    `.omo/ulw-loop/019ed2ae-8d4b-7123-97c5-006b6d494778/goals.json`; durable root plan was read directly.

### Hypotheses

1. [OPEN] `sp70` is filled from a stale pointer or object field before `0x004d7a7b`, not from the clicked grid cell.
   Distinguishing evidence: hook immediately before `0x004d7a7b` shows stack/local value source and the first write to
   `state+0x24`. If true, fix is: source writer.
2. [OPEN] `DAT_007cd04c+0x11178/+0x1117c` current/list remain zero, so projection uses camera/default object state and
   loses X. Distinguishing evidence: runtime watch around `FUN_004b25a0` or root current/list writer shows no valid current
   object before click. If true, fix is: current import.
3. [OPEN] visible star labels are rendered from marker table, but SelectGrid hit-test uses a different coordinate frame or
   target table. Distinguishing evidence: click path sees marker render coords but target validator args derive from a
   separate table not populated by `0x0313/0x0315`. If true, fix is: target frame.

- [x] UI explorer session `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-selectgrid-upstream-v52-47900-20260618`.

- [x] Evidence files `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-upstream-v52-20260618.*`.
  Cleanup: kept as evidence. Broad upstream watcher is noisy, but useful as a negative/gating lesson.

  Cleanup: verify no `G7MTClient.exe`, `frida.exe`, or watcher Python remains.
- [x] Port `47900` listener spawned by UI explorer.
  Cleanup: verify no `LISTENING` entry on `4787`, `47900`, `47901`.

### Findings

- 2026-06-18 star-slot recheck: user challenged the “only one blue star” visual read. Re-sampled installed
  assets under `.omo/work/logh7-installed/data`: `fs_glow_000..006` / `fs000_f..fs006_f` are ordered
  blue-violet, blue, blue-white/cyan, yellow, orange, red-orange, red. This supports the current render
  mapping `O/B/A/F/G/K/M -> byte2 0/1/2/3/4/5/6`. The data histogram remains `O=2,B=5,A=7,F=8,G=19,K=17,M=21`;
  per-named-system class remains provisional because `Null_galaxy.mdx star_<NN>_<class>` is not directly linked
  to `content/galaxy.json` system names. Evidence: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-star-slot-texture-contact-20260618.png`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-p002-star-spectral-variant-20260618.md`.
- 2026-06-18 v52 runtime: after minimap navigation, screenshot
  `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-selectgrid-upstream-v52-47900-20260618/shots/005-v52-minimap-right.png`
  showed `베큘라` as orange/yellow and `발할라` as cyan/blue in the same viewport. This supports the
  star-slot/color correction, but does not prove per-name original spectral classes because the join remains
  `model_node_order_provisional`.
- v52 visible-star clicks did not complete C002. Left-clicking `발할라` around `(1100,311)` produced only
  `0x0300->0x0301`; right-clicking `발할라` and left-clicking `베큘라` produced no strategic command trace.
  No native `0x0b01` or `0x0b07` equivalent was observed.
- Static v52 disassembly shows `FUN_004d3580` reads world vector X/Z and writes both grid X/Y. It is not an
  X-omitting function. Evidence: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-upstream-static-v52-20260618.md`.
- Runtime v52 split: the broad upstream watcher was not click-gated and mostly captured mouse `(757,997)`,
  so it cannot be used as the star-click cause. It did prove one live branch where `FUN_004b25a0` produced
  world `(34.2525,0,-6.7349)` and `FUN_004d3580` output grid `(84,31)`. The state watcher is the click evidence:
  `발할라` click mouse `(1098,308)` yielded world `(37.5093,0,-0.5053)` and projected `(x=0x007b360c,y=25)`;
  `베큘라` click mouse `(470,140)` yielded world `(31.4896,0,1.5024)` and projected `(x=0x007b360c,y=23)`.
  `FUN_004d6310` returned `-256` in both cases. Root current/list stayed
  `DAT_007cd04c+0x11178=0`, `+0x1117c=0`; command state stayed `selectedD5=-1`, `categoryD6=-1`.
- 판정: C002는 pending. 다음은 보이는 항성 클릭 반복이 아니라 `DAT_007cd04c+0x11178/+0x1117c`
  writer, state `p24ProjX` source/caller local, 그리고 `selectedD5/categoryD6` action-state writer를
  정적/런타임 양쪽에서 추적한다. Evidence:
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-upstream-v52-20260618.md`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-state-v52-20260618.jsonl`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-upstream-v52-20260618.jsonl`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-upstream-v52-cleanup-20260618.txt`.

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v53 static source/writer correction

- 목표: v52의 visible star click 실패를 클릭 반복 없이 정적 callsite와 source/current import chain으로
  재검증한다. 사용자 지적대로 항성 타입도 다시 분리해, 다색 렌더 판정과 이름별 등급 확정을 혼동하지
  않는다.
- 항성 타입 판정: `content/extracted/model-galaxy-stars.json` 기준 분포는
  `O=2,B=5,A=7,F=8,G=19,K=17,M=21`이고 설치 텍스처 `fs_glow_000..006` /
  `fs000_f..fs006_f`는 청자색, 청색, 청백/청록, 황색, 주황, 적주황, 적색 슬롯이다.
  따라서 "파란 항성 하나뿐"은 틀렸다. 단, `Null_galaxy.mdx star_<NN>_<class>`와
  `content/galaxy.json` 성계명의 직접 연결은 계속 `model_node_order_provisional`이다.
- Hypothesis H1 result: static projection callsite is sane. `0x004d7a6c..0x004d7b13`은
  world local, yOut, xOut을 `FUN_004d3580`에 넘기고, return 뒤 xOut/yOut을
  `state+0x24/+0x28`에 복사한 뒤 `FUN_004d6310`에 넣는다. `FUN_004d3580`도 X/Z를
  둘 다 grid X/Y로 쓴다. v52의 `state.p24ProjX=0x007b360c`는 정적 X-omitting 버그가
  아니라 클릭 순간 caller local, watcher timing, 또는 upstream value source 문제다.
- Hypothesis H2 result: current/list writer chain is narrowed to optional record `+0x08`.
  직접 절대 참조 스캔에서 `DAT_007cd04c`, `DAT_009d2a30`, `DAT_00c9eabc`,
  `DAT_00c9eac0` 관련 write는 0건이었다. v41/v45 기준 current/focus source는
  `FUN_004b5bb0([mainState+8]) -> source+0x320`이고, 이 값은 `0x004c2c80` import path의
  optional record `+0x08`에서 복사되지만 현재 optional record `+0x08`은 0이다.
- Hypothesis H3 result: command confirmation positive-control is not a fix. `FUN_00570a10`
  의 `DAT_009d2a3c==2` branch가 confirm과 `0x0b01`을 여는 것은 v14b에서 증명됐지만,
  자연 writer와 유효 `DAT_009d2a40` 목적지는 아직 없다.
- 판정: C002는 pending. 다음 runtime은 visible star click 좌표에 한정해 `FUN_004d3580`
  entry/leave와 `0x004d7a80/8c/9c/b13` local/state 값을 같은 event id로 묶고,
  별도 pass에서 optional record `+0x08` writer/origin 및 `이미 탈퇴하셨습니다.` UI message
  source를 추적한다.
- Evidence: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-source-static-v53-20260618.md`.

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v54 click-gated projection writepoint correction

- 목표: 사용자 지적대로 항성 타입을 다시 재검산하고, 보이는 `발할라`/`베큘라` 클릭이
  실제 grid X/Y projection을 만드는지 함수-entry hook 대신 writepoint로 확인한다.
- 항성 타입 판정: 검산 agent와 root 재검산 모두 `content/extracted/model-galaxy-stars.json`
  histogram `O=2,B=5,A=7,F=8,G=19,K=17,M=21` 및 설치 텍스처
  `fs_glow_000..006` / `fs000_f..fs006_f` 7슬롯을 확인했다. "파란색 하나"는 틀렸다.
  단, 성계명별 등급 join은 계속 `model_node_order_provisional`이다.
- Runtime session: `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-selectgrid-v54-47900-20260618`, canonical playable
  SHA `e75486ef762787448d91e38a612103f6d11691833c36a6bcb30d13a9cbdb2366`.
  월드 진입 trace는 `0x0206`, `0x0305`, `0x0313`, `0x0315`, `0x0325`, `0x0323`,
  `0x0f06->0x0f07`, `0x0b09`, `0x0b0a`, `0x0356`, `0x1200/1202/1201`을 포함한다.
- 화면 증거: `shots/005-v54-minimap-right.png`에서 `베큘라`는 주황/황색,
  `발할라`는 청색/청록으로 같은 viewport에 보인다. 이는 다색 항성 렌더 증거지만,
  이름별 원본 분광형 확정은 아니다.
- Hook correction: `FUN_004d3580` entry hook은 stack/prologue 관측에 취약해 폐기했다.
  `0x004d359c` X write hook은 runtime에서 설치/발화했고, `0x004d35aa` 및
  `0x004d35ac`는 Frida가 `unable to intercept function`으로 거부했다. 최종 watcher는
  Y pre-write 지점 `0x004d35a6`에서 `eax` value와 `[esp+0x0c]` target pointer를 읽는다.
  Focused tests `python -m unittest tools.tests.test_logh7_selectgrid_upstream_watch
  tools.tests.test_logh7_selectgrid_state_watch` passed 8 tests; py_compile passed.
- Runtime writepoint evidence: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-upstream-v54-writepoint-prep-20260618.jsonl`
  recorded `hook-installed=5`, `hook-failed=0`, `gridProjector-write-x-004d359c=2`,
  `gridProjector-write-y-prep-004d35a6=2`, and `projection-call-after-004d7a80=2`.
  `발할라` click `(1179,448)` produced world `(35.59025955200195,0,2.466439723968506)`
  and grid `(85,22)`. `베큘라` click `(518,264)` produced world
  `(29.58106231689453,0,4.468449592590332)` and grid `(79,20)`.
- Server trace result: these visible star clicks still do not complete C002. Trace remains
  heartbeat/info path (`0x0300->0x0301` or `0x0f08->0x0f09`), with no inbound `0x0b01`
  or outbound `0x0b07`.
- Cleanup: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-v54-cleanup-20260618.txt` shows
  UI explorer stopped, installed client SHA restored to
  `e75486ef762787448d91e38a612103f6d11691833c36a6bcb30d13a9cbdb2366`, and no residual
  game/Frida/watcher process or `4787/47900/47901` listener.
- 판정: C002 remains pending. Next discriminator is not another visible-star click; trace
  `FUN_004d6310` validator, root current/list writer, `DAT_007cd04c+0x11178/+0x1117c`,
  and `selectedD5/categoryD6` transition for grid `(85,22)` / `(79,20)` under one click event id.
- Evidence: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-v54-runtime-20260618.md`.

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v55 SelectGrid click-correlation callsite split

- 목표: 사용자가 지적한 항성 타입 오판을 재확인하고, v54에서 확인한 visible-star grid
  `(85,22)` / `(79,20)`가 실제 validator/current/command state로 이어지지 않는 지점을
  한 click id로 묶는다.
- 항성 타입 판정: `content/extracted/model-galaxy-stars.json`은 계속
  `O=2,B=5,A=7,F=8,G=19,K=17,M=21`이고, O/B만 7개라 "파란 항성 하나"는 틀렸다.
  이름별 원본 등급은 여전히 `model_node_order_provisional`이다.
- Tooling: `tools/logh7_selectgrid_click_correlation_watch.py`와
  `tools/tests/test_logh7_selectgrid_click_correlation_watch.py`를 추가했다. Focused
  unittest 3개, 기존 upstream/state watcher 포함 11개, py_compile 모두 통과했다.
  watcher pure LOC는 247, test는 70이다.
- Runtime session: `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-selectgrid-v55-47900-20260618`,
  canonical playable SHA `e75486ef762787448d91e38a612103f6d11691833c36a6bcb30d13a9cbdb2366`.
  `shots/004-v55-minimap-right.png`에서 `베큘라`는 주황/황색, `발할라`는 청색/청록으로
  보인다. 월드 진입 trace는 `0x0206`, `0x0305`, `0x0313`, `0x0315`, `0x0325`,
  `0x0323`, `0x0f01`, `0x0f03`, `0x0f06->0x0f07`, `0x0b09`, `0x0b0a`, `0x0356`,
  `0x1200/1202/1201`을 포함했다.
- Runtime evidence: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-click-correlation-v55-realcall-20260618.jsonl`
  에서 `hook-installed=9`, `hook-failed=0`, `click-start=1`,
  `gridProjector-write-x-004d359c=1`, `gridProjector-write-y-prep-004d35a6=1`,
  `validator-callsite-before-004d7bba=1`, `targetValidator-enter/leave=1/1`을 기록했다.
  `발할라` click `(1179,448)`의 writepoint path는 grid `(85,22)`였지만 실제 validator
  분기는 오래 보던 `0x004d7b13`이 아니라 lower branch `0x004d7bba`였다. 그 callsite는
  `sp00=8074780=0x007b361c`, `sp04=22`, `sp08=0xffffffff`를 push했고
  `FUN_004d6310`은 `-256`을 반환했다. pass branch `0x004d7bc3`은 0회였다.
  `DAT_007cd04c+0x11178/+0x1117c`는 `0/0`, `selectedD5/categoryD6`는 `-1/-1`로
  남았다.
- Static discriminator: disasm of `0x004d7a6c..0x004d7bbf` confirms
  `0x004d7a7b` calls `FUN_004d3580`; before `add esp,0xc`, `0x004d7a84` reads
  `[esp+0x70]` and `0x004d7a88` reads `[esp+0x6c]`; `0x004d7a8c/0x004d7a9c`
  copy those values into `state+0x24/+0x28`; lower branch `0x004d7bae..0x004d7bba`
  pushes `state+0x24`, `state+0x28`, `-1` into `FUN_004d6310`, and `0x004d7bbf`
  tests `AL`.
- 판정: C002 pending. Fresh client next run must use the updated correlation watcher to capture
  `projectionStack`, `projectorWriteArgs`, and `projection-state-written-after-004d7aa9`.
  The post-update pass could not run in v55 because the client had already closed with
  `ECONNRESET`.
- Cleanup: UI explorer stop restored installed client SHA
  `e75486ef762787448d91e38a612103f6d11691833c36a6bcb30d13a9cbdb2366`; residual checks found
  no game/Frida/watcher process and no `4787/47900/47901` listener.
- Evidence: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-v55-click-correlation-20260618.md`.

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v56 SelectGrid post-copy state proof

- 목표: v55가 요구한 `projectionStack`, `projectorWriteArgs`,
  `projection-state-written-after-004d7aa9`를 fresh client에서 수집하고, 사용자가 다시
  지적한 항성 타입/색상 오판을 증거로 정리한다.
- 항성 타입 판정: `content/extracted/model-galaxy-stars.json`은
  `O=2,B=5,A=7,F=8,G=19,K=17,M=21`이다. O/B만 7개라 "파란색 하나"는 틀렸다.
  실클라 v56 화면에서도 `베큘라`는 주황/황색, `발할라`는 청색/청록으로 보였다.
  단, 성계명별 원본 등급은 여전히 `model_node_order_provisional`이다.
- 런타임 세션: `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-selectgrid-v56-47900-20260618`,
  canonical playable SHA `e75486ef762787448d91e38a612103f6d11691833c36a6bcb30d13a9cbdb2366`.
  첫 캐릭터 선택은 빈 로비 상태였고, game-start retry 후 카드가 보인 상태에서 선택해
  월드/HUD에 들어갔다. 미니맵 이동 후 `shots/009-v56-minimap-right-world.png`에서
  `베큘라`/`발할라` 색상 차이를 확인했다.
- Watcher 시도: v56 copy/ready/starcenter 파일 3개는 hook/heartbeat만 남긴
  타이밍/좌표 실패 증거다. 성공 파일은
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-click-correlation-v56-long-20260618.jsonl`.
  counts는 `hook-installed=10`, `watch-ready=1`, `watch-heartbeat=123`,
  `click-start=1`, `worldProjector-leave=1`, `projection-call-before=1`,
  `gridProjector-write-x=1`, `gridProjector-write-y-prep=1`,
  `projection-call-after=1`, `projection-state-written-after-004d7aa9=1`,
  `validator-callsite-before-004d7bba=1`, `targetValidator-enter/leave=1/1`이다.
- 런타임 증거: `발할라` 중심 클릭 `(723,545)`은 world
  `(37.525245666503906,0,-0.4923539161682129)`로 투영됐다. `FUN_004d3580`
  writepoint는 X `87`, Y `25`를 만들었다. 그러나 `0x004d7a80` 뒤 stack은
  `sp70=8074780`, `sp6c=25`였고, `0x004d7aa9` 직후 `state+0x24/+0x28`도
  `8074780/25`였다. 실제 `0x004d7bba` callsite는 `sp00=8074780=0x007b361c`,
  `sp04=25`, `sp08=0xffffffff`를 push했고, `FUN_004d6310`은 `-256`을 반환했다.
- 서버 trace 결과: 보이는 항성 클릭은 아직 `0x0300->0x0301`과 `0x0f08->0x0f09`만
  만들었다. 자연 inbound `0x0b01`과 outbound `0x0b07`은 없다.
- 정리: UI explorer stop은 설치 클라이언트 SHA를
  `e75486ef762787448d91e38a612103f6d11691833c36a6bcb30d13a9cbdb2366`로 복구했고
  `shaVerified=true`를 보고했다. 프로세스 확인에서는 잔여 `G7MTClient`/Frida/Python watcher가
  없었고, 포트 확인에서도 `4787/47900/47901` listener가 없었다.
- 판정: C002 pending. 다음은 항성 색/클릭 도달 반복이 아니라 `0x004d7a80` 전후의
  `sp70` source/caller local writer다. `FUN_004d3580` writepoint grid X는 정상에
  가깝지만 state-copy가 validator X로 pointer-like `0x007b361c`를 흘린다.
- 증거: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-v56-copy-state-20260618.md`.

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v57 SelectGrid sp70 source probe 시작

- 목표: v56이 증명한 `FUN_004d3580` writepoint grid `(87,25)`와
  state-copy 직후 `state+0x24=0x007b361c`의 불일치를 더 이상 항성 색상/클릭 도달
  문제로 보지 않는다. 이번 루프는 `0x004d7a80` 전후 caller local `sp70`이 언제
  pointer-like 값으로 채워지는지 판별한다.
- 가설 H1: `sp70`은 `0x004d7a7b` 직전부터 stale pointer/object field로 채워져 있고,
  `FUN_004d3580` writepoint의 정상 X 값은 다른 stack/local에 기록된다.
  판별 증거는 `0x004d7a70/75/7a/7b/80/84/8c/aa9`의 stack window와 xOut/yOut
  pointer/value 동시 기록이다.
- 가설 H2: `FUN_004d3580`이 정상 X를 `[esp+0x70]`에 써야 하지만 hook 시점의
  `esp` 기준 해석이 caller/callee 전환 때문에 어긋나 있다. 판별 증거는
  `0x004d359c` X write target pointer와 caller의 `[esp+0x70]` 주소가 동일한지,
  그리고 return 직후 `[esp+0x70]` 값이 실제로 바뀌었는지다.
- 가설 H3: `0x004d7a80` 이후 copy 경계에서 다른 branch 또는 register carry가
  `state+0x24`를 덮어쓴다. 판별 증거는 `0x004d7a84/88/8c/9c/aa9`에서
  `eax/ecx/ebp`, `state+0x24/+0x28`, stack window가 순서대로 변하는 로그다.
- Tooling decision: `tools/logh7_selectgrid_click_correlation_watch.py`는 pure LOC 247이라
  더 키우지 않는다. v57은 read-only 전용 `sp70` source watcher를 별도 파일로 만든다.
  되돌림 기준은 새 watcher/test/evidence 문서 제거이며, 기존 v55/v56 증거와 watcher는
  건드리지 않는다.

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v57-v60 SelectGrid return-gated correction

- Source: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-sp70-source-v57e-safe-20260618.jsonl`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-sp70-source-v58-return-gated-20260618.jsonl`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-selectgrid-click-correlation-v59-return-gated-20260618.jsonl`,
  `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-selectgrid-v60-natural-47900-20260618/shots/006-v60-natural-click-valhalla.png`,
  static disassembly of `0x004d3580`, `0x004d7a6c..0x004d7bbf`, `0x004d6310`,
  and `0x004d35b0`.
- Tooling correction: Frida hooks on x86 call instructions are unsafe here.
  Hooking `0x004d7a7b` changed the callee return address from `0x004d7a80`
  to trampoline `0x512062f` and made the X out target look like `0x512061f`.
  Therefore v55/v56 `state+0x24=0x007b361c` is no longer treated as a natural
  projection/copy-state fact.
- Fixed probe: `tools/logh7_selectgrid_sp70_source_watch.py` now uses
  `0x004d3581` after `push esi`, gated by `returnAddress == 0x004d7a80`.
  v58 produced 28 matching projection entries: `xOutPtr=0x19fc98`,
  X write target `0x19fc98`, X values `87/88/89/90`, and Y `25`. After-call
  and copy-state values matched those grid coordinates.
- Correlation probe correction: `tools/logh7_selectgrid_click_correlation_watch.py`
  removed the `0x004d7a7b` call hook and later removed validator-near Frida
  hooks (`0x004d7bb8`, `0x004d7bba`, `0x004d7bbf`, `0x004d7bc3`, `0x004d6310`)
  because v58/v59 showed they perturb or crash the client.
- Runtime/static validator evidence: v59 reached `selectedCell=(87,25)`,
  `cellValue=73`, object bytes `(17,3,1)`, current raw/list `0/0`,
  `selectedD5/categoryD6=-1/-1` before the unsafe validator hook killed the
  client. Static `FUN_004d35b0` returns object byte `+1`, so object1 `3`
  passes the first `FUN_004d6310` gate; range `-1` reaches the success path.
- Natural QA: v60 used no Frida hook for the star click. Login, character select,
  world entry, minimap navigation, and `발할라` click completed with
  `clientAlive=true`. The screenshot shows the blue/cyan `발할라` cell highlighted.
  The server trace only added `0x0300->0x0301`; no `0x0b01/0x0b07` command loop
  yet.
- Star type clarification: visible `베큘라` remains orange/yellow and `발할라`
  blue/cyan; static star distribution remains `O=2,B=5,A=7,F=8,G=19,K=17,M=21`.
  Name-specific spectral class is still provisional.
- Verification: `python -m py_compile tools/logh7_selectgrid_sp70_source_watch.py tools/logh7_selectgrid_click_correlation_watch.py`
  passed, and `python -m unittest tools.tests.test_logh7_selectgrid_sp70_source_watch tools.tests.test_logh7_selectgrid_click_correlation_watch tools.tests.test_logh7_selectgrid_upstream_watch tools.tests.test_logh7_selectgrid_state_watch`
  ran 15 tests OK.
- 판정: C002 pending. Projection and validator are not the next blocker. The
  next cycle should trace post-selection command/action state after a highlighted
  valid star cell, preferably with static analysis or guarded file-backed probes
  instead of Frida hooks near call instructions.

## 2026-06-18 - G006 C002 v61 command/action xref 및 정보 패널 확인

- `tools/logh7_disasm_range.py`에 절대 메모리 xref 스캔을 추가했다.
  `0x0057bbc0:+0x260` 범위에서 `DAT_00c9eabc/eac0` read xref
  `0x0057bc87`, `0x0057bc95`, `0x0057bca0`를 잡는 unittest가 통과한다.
- Ghidra `functions.jsonl` 함수 시작 주소를 기준으로 `.text` 전체 함수 범위를
  스캔한 결과, `DAT_00c9eabc`, `DAT_00c9eac0`는 모두 read이고 direct write는
  0건이었다. 주소 자체가 immediate로 전달되는 곳도 `c9eabc/eac0`는 없었다.
- root 구조체 직접 displacement 스캔에서도 `DAT_007cd04c+0x11178/+0x1117c/+0x11180`
  write는 잡히지 않았고 `+0x11178` read 및 `lea root+0x11174`만 확인됐다.
- 정적 판정: command renderer `0x0057bbc0`는 root action list count와
  `DAT_00c9eabc/eac0` 선택 전역을 읽어서 행을 그린다. `0x0057bd90`/`0x0057c250`
  계열은 `esi+0x15a8` UI container 내부 목록을 별도로 그린다. 따라서 하이라이트된
  항성 셀만으로 command/action list가 채워진다는 가정은 폐기한다.
- 실클라 v61에서 하단 우측 정보 아이콘과 정보 패널 캐릭터 행을 클릭했다.
  자연 trace는 `0x0f06->0x0f07` 및 extra `0x0b09`, `0x0325`, `0x0323`,
  `0x0b0a`, `0x0356`, `0x1200/1202/1201` 재전송을 만들었지만 `0x0b01/0x0b07`은
  만들지 않았다.
- UI 판정: `shots/011-011-click-bottom-icon-2.png`는 월드 위 정보 패널에
  `접속하고 싶은 캐릭터를 선택해 주세요.`, `NO DATA`, `???`가 남은 것을 보인다.
  이는 UI 문맥/한글화 미완료 증거다.
- 다음 목표: 항성 색상/projection 반복 금지. `0x0323/0x0356` payload 또는 네이티브
  mode/category 조작이 UI/root action container를 채우는 경계를 추적한다.

## 2026-06-20 - G006 C002 focus-cell + postload unit stream live result

- Baseline rerun (`g006-c002-current-bootstrap-20260620b`) reproduced the current failure:
  `0x0356` arrived with `recordSeatCount250=1`, but the visible HUD still showed `* NO DATA`
  and clicks produced only `0x0300/0x0301` or postload refresh traffic.
- `source_import_watch` on the baseline captured the old root cause in current bits:
  early/native `0x0325` parsed as `unitCount41a364=256`, while postload import still had
  `primaryRecord.optionalRecordPlus08=0`, `unit0.optionalRecordPlus08=1` only in the misparsed
  native table, and `sourceFields.predictedSource320=0`.
- `LOGH_POSTLOAD_UNIT_STREAM_WIRE=1` corrected the postload unit table in the server trace:
  `unitCountBe0=1`, `unit0IdBe2=1`. Native watcher then showed `unitCount41a364=1`,
  `primaryRecord.recordId0=1`, `primaryRecord.primaryUnit24=1`, but `primaryRecord.optionalRecordPlus08=0`
  and `source320=0`.
- `LOGH_PLAYER_FOCUS_CELL=1` plus postload parser-stream advanced the root current path:
  `logh7_root_init_watch` captured `DAT_007cd04c != null`, `currentRaw11178=2550`, `currentX=50`,
  `currentY=25` in `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-focuscell-root-watch-20260620.jsonl`.
  This proves the server-side focus-cell seed can populate the root current cell without the rejected
  global `strat-source-mode` patch.
- C002 is still not passed. With `currentRaw11178=2550`, natural clicks on the current/adjacent
  central grid candidates, hardware `F`, and right-click still produced no inbound `0x0b01` and no
  outbound `0x0b07`; observed post-probe traffic was `0x0300/0x0301` plus one `0x0f08/0x0f09`
  information path. Screenshot `shots/005-focuscell-click-east-cell.png` still shows the lower-left
  action list as `* NO DATA`.
- Implementation change from this evidence: promote `LOGH_POSTLOAD_UNIT_STREAM_WIRE=1` and
  `LOGH_PLAYER_FOCUS_CELL=1` into playable defaults and launcher env. Narrow tests pass in both
  root and split-server trees:
  `node --test tests/server/logh7-config.test.mjs tests/server/logh7-login-session.test.mjs`;
  `node --test server/tests/server/logh7-config.test.mjs server/tests/server/logh7-login-session.test.mjs`.
- Next target: not projection/color and not raw coordinate repeats. Trace the post-current command/action
  admission path: runtime command containers, SelectGrid/category state, and the natural writer that moves
  the UI toward `DAT_009d2a3c=2` or equivalent `0x0b01` emission.

## 2026-06-20 — GDI font face was Pretendard, but quality still looked legacy

- User-visible symptom: "아직 폰트는 시스템 폰트 그대론거 같던데."
- Byte verification showed the global face slot at file offset `0x0037402c` was already
  `50726574656e64617264000000000000` (`Pretendard`) in the canonical playable and client vendor
  EXEs. Therefore the remaining visual issue was not the face string alone.
- GDI probe on the host showed `CreateFontA(face='Pretendard', charset=0x81)` resolves to
  `Pretendard`. `Pretendard JP` resolves to `굴림` under `HANGEUL_CHARSET`, so the EXE face must
  stay `Pretendard`; JP/Std remain distribution payloads, not the client face.
- RE-confirmed the two font creation sites still pushed `ANTIALIASED_QUALITY`:
  `FUN_004aec70` at VA `0x004aeddc`, and `FUN_004b0960` at VA `0x004b0b91`.
- Added `tools/client_patches/font-cleartype.json`, changing both immediates `6a04` -> `6a05`
  (`CLEARTYPE_QUALITY`). `font-cleartype` is now in the default playable stack after `font-face`.
- New canonical playable SHA256 after deploy:
  `15ed8a35ea3891374096b25d43878e74a6abbf97242b32ecf357ca4c577768e0`.
- Synced the exact EXE into `.omo/work/logh7-installed/exe/G7MTClient.exe`,
  `.omo/work/logh7-installed/exe/G7MTClient.exe.uiexplorer`,
  `client/vendor/logh7-installed/exe/G7MTClient.exe`, and
  `client/vendor/logh7-installed/exe/G7MTClient.exe.uiexplorer`.
- Regression:
  `python -m unittest tools.tests.test_logh7_client_exe tools.tests.test_logh7_installed_tree tools.tests.test_logh7_japanese_font_patch`
  passed; `client/` `npm run check:package` passed.

## 2026-06-20 - G006 C002 command-admission path narrowed upstream of SelectGrid

- User directive: continue client RE and document continuously; manual features and formerly-unimplemented features must all be made playable.
- Static RE result: current-cell/focus/unit stream work is necessary but not sufficient for natural movement. The remaining path is:
  selection payload import -> selection row hit-test -> HUD category apply -> command row build -> command row hit -> SelectGrid factory.
- `FUN_004f68f0(selectionList,payload)` writes `selectionList+0x628 = payload`, reads `payload+0x270`, and writes the count to
  `selectionList+0x620` (`listCount188`).
- `FUN_004f6600(selectionList)` loops row object pointers at `selectionList+(0x22+i)*4` and `selectionList+(0x32+i)*4`,
  tests each with `FUN_005015f0`, and writes `selectionList+0x624` (`listSelected189`) on hit.
- `FUN_004fd100(HUD)` only enters the category application path when `HUD+0xf4 == 2` and `HUD+0xab0` changes during the tick.
  It then calls `FUN_004f6b00` and `FUN_004f5cb0`.
- `FUN_004f6b00(selectionList)` returns `*(u16 *)(payload + 0x26c + (listCount - selectedIndex) * 8)` for
  `0 <= selectedIndex < 0x10`, else `0xffffffff`.
- `FUN_004f5cb0(commandMenu,category)` reads the command table returned by `FUN_004c8700()` (`clientBase+0x3416d8`),
  sets `commandMenu+0x358 = category` (`index 0xd6`) and `commandMenu+0x350 = rowCount` (`index 0xd4`).
- `FUN_004f58c0(commandMenu,outFlag)` hit-tests command rows and calls `FUN_004f93c0(factoryIndex,category)`.
  `FUN_00581c80` remains the SelectGrid factory (`factoryIndex=0x2b`) and constructs the `0x0b01` send /
  `0x0b07` receive result path.
- Implementation: `tools/logh7_selectgrid_snapshot.py` now dumps `hudModeF4`, `hudState14e0`, selection row
  primary/secondary gate/id/rects, command row gate/id/rects, `listSelected189`, and command category state without hooks.
- Regression: `python -m unittest tools.tests.test_logh7_selectgrid_snapshot` passed; `python -m py_compile
  tools/logh7_selectgrid_snapshot.py tools/tests/test_logh7_selectgrid_snapshot.py` passed. Pure LOC stays below 250
  for the touched script.
- Evidence doc: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-command-admission-re-20260620.md`.

## 2026-06-20 - G006 C002 HUD command-admission live result

- Session `session-g006-c002-hud-admission-20260620c` reached the real strategic world with canonical playable
  SHA `15ed8a35ea3891374096b25d43878e74a6abbf97242b32ecf357ca4c577768e0` after disabling strict
  account DB. Follow-up analysis corrected the earlier strict-DB suspicion: the throwaway account file
  verified against `ginei00/dummy ` (trailing space), not `ginei00/dummy`. The reject was caused by the
  ad hoc shell stdin command that created the evidence DB, not by SQLite/authentication itself.
- Baseline snapshot: `payloadCount270=1`, `listCount188=1`, selection row objects exist, command row objects
  exist (`rowCountD4=24`), `root.currentRaw11178=2550`, and link state has one character plus one unit.
  This refutes missing world/player/focus-cell as the immediate C002 blocker in this run.
- Natural input result:
  center marker click changed only projection/cell selection; selection row candidate `(80,795)` produced one
  client-origin `0x0f08` and server `0x0f09` `respLen=7`; command-row coordinate probes `(57,146)` and
  `(57,910)` produced no `0x0b01`/`0x0b07`.
- Admission state stayed blocked: `hudModeF4=1`, `hudAb0=-1`, `listSelected189=-1`,
  `categoryD6=-1`, `selectedD5=-1`. Runtime table snapshot showed `table305.commandCount14=0`,
  `table307.commandCount14=3`.
- Verdict: C002 remains FAIL. The fresh blocker is not star color, coordinate projection, root current,
  or command-row click location. It is the natural writer path that should move the HUD from selection
  payload/import into category application (`hudModeF4=2`, nonnegative `hudAb0`, nonnegative
  `listSelected189`) and then into the correct command table. The observed `0x0f08->0x0f09`
  is also a useful separate lead for the empty info-panel/system/planet data problem because the server
  currently answers it with only a 7-byte status object.

## 2026-06-20 - Account admin stdin footgun fixed after C002 strict-DB correction

- Diagnosis: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-hud-admission-accounts-20260620.json` contained account
  `ginei00`, but `createAccountStore(...).authenticate(buildGin7Credential({account:'ginei00',password:'dummy'}))`
  returned `authentication failed`. Brute-force candidate verification showed the persisted hash matched
  password `dummy ` with a trailing space.
- Fix: `src/server/logh7-admin.mjs` now rejects client login passwords whose trimmed value differs from the
  submitted value and reports `password must be 1-8 printable ASCII characters without surrounding spaces`.
  `tools/launcher/LOGH7Launcher.cs` and `tools/standalone/signup-portal/serve.py` mirror the same validation
  and Korean message.
- Regression: focused `node --test --test-name-pattern "passwords the real client|surrounding spaces|stdin without password argv" tests/server/logh7-admin.test.mjs`
  passed; `python -m py_compile tools/standalone/signup-portal/serve.py` passed; `python -m unittest
  tools.tests.test_logh7_installed_tree` passed.

## 2026-06-20 - G006 C002 0x0f08 diagnostic word summary

- Added a conservative parser for diagnostic trace only: `src/server/logh7-auth-server.mjs` now records
  `innerPayloadWordsBeHex` and `innerPayloadNonzeroWordsBe` for non-credential `0x0f08` messages.
  Credential opcodes `0x7000` and `0x2000` still expose no raw payload hex.
- For the strict live payload
  `0f080000000100000000000000000000000000000000000000000101`, the derived BE words are:
  `0x0f08, 0x0000, 0x0001, 0x0000, 0x0000, 0x0000, 0x0000, 0x0000, 0x0000, 0x0000, 0x0000, 0x0000, 0x0000, 0x0101`.
  Nonzero words are offset `0` (`0x0f08`), offset `4` (`0x0001`), and offset `26` (`0x0101`).
- Static RE tie-in:
  `FUN_004b78a0` switches on `(param_3 & 0xffff) - 1`; runtime `param_3=0x45` therefore lands in
  decompile `case 0x44`, which maps request `0x0f08` to response `0x0f09`. The packer records `param_4`
  and the request/expected-response pair in the pending ring when `param_2 != 0`, or sends immediately when
  `param_2 == 0`.
- Regression:
  red test `node --test --test-name-pattern "0x0f08 diagnostic payload words" tests/server/logh7-auth-server.test.mjs`
  failed before implementation; focused green passed 3 tests; `node --check` passed for changed `.mjs` files;
  `npm run test:server` passed 1062 tests.
- Limitation:
  the new summary is deterministic decoding of the already live-captured payload. A fresh real-client run has
  not yet been made after adding the word-summary fields.

- Static RE was rechecked around the native strategic-command admission path:

  row hit-test, `FUN_004fd100` is the per-frame HUD gate, `FUN_004fd7a0` writes `hud+0xf4`, `FUN_004f6b00`
  resolves the selected category, `FUN_004f5cb0` builds the command menu, `FUN_004f58c0` scans command rows,
  `FUN_004f93c0` dispatches the row factory, and `FUN_00581c80` creates the SelectGrid send/receive object
  for `0x0b01` / `0x0b07`.

  attach-only/read-only: it hooks the nine admission functions above and arms `MemoryAccessMonitor` write watches

  fields are deliberately de-duplicated because the live client showed they alias the same runtime address.

  `FUN_004fd7a0`, `FUN_004f6b00`, `FUN_004f5cb0`, `FUN_004f93c0`, or `FUN_00581c80`, and no watched field

  validation. `FUN_005025f0` is the rectangle test, with optional `+0x0c/+0x10` offsets gated by bytes

## 2026-06-21 - G006 C002 mode-target gate classification

- Read-only session `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-c002-mode-target-state-20260621c/` captured 18,630
  `FUN_005015f0` leaves with `retvalLow8=0` for every observed target. The four HUD mode targets stayed
  `valid08=1`, had stable rects and empty event queues, and all had `gate05=0`; fallback targets also had
  `flag15=1`.
- Static RE confirms the immediate predicate: `FUN_005024a0` returns object byte `+5`, `FUN_005024b0` writes
  byte `+5`, and `FUN_005015f0` rejects before rect/occlusion checks when `+5` is zero. The current C002
  blocker is disabled target gate, not command row geometry.
- Explicit debug force session `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-c002-force-gate-20260621d/` wrote
  `hudTarget24-mode6-fallback +5` from `0` to `1` once. This did not open C002: all captured low bytes stayed
  zero, trace had no `0x0b01`/`0x0b07`, and the client ended with `read ECONNRESET`. Single-byte `+5` forcing
  is therefore an unsafe non-fix.
- `tools/logh7_hud_admission_watch.py` now keeps default operation read-only, exposes the force behavior only
  behind `--force-interaction-target-gate`, and preserves evidence when the target process exits before Frida
  unload by reporting cleanup errors in JSON output.
- Evidence: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-input-gate-classification-20260621d.md`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-mode-target-state-summary-20260621c.json`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-force-gate-summary-20260621d.json`.
  Verification: `python -m unittest tools.tests.test_logh7_hud_admission_watch` passed 5 tests and
  `python -m py_compile tools\logh7_hud_admission_watch.py tools\tests\test_logh7_hud_admission_watch.py`
  passed.

## 2026-06-21 - G006 C002 this-context gate correction

- Static correction:
  the first `FUN_005015f0` `+5` predicate is not the target object's byte. Disassembly shows
  `0x00501600 mov esi, ecx`, `0x0050163e mov ecx, esi`, `0x00501640 call 0x5024a0`, and
  `0x005024a0 mov al, byte ptr [ecx+5]`; therefore the immediate early-return gate is
  `thisEcx+5`. The target pointer is the stack arg saved in `ebx` and is checked later through
  `FUN_005025c0`, which reads `target+0x15`.
- Mode table:
  PE bytes at `DAT_006703c0` show `FUN_004fd7a0` mode tables such as mode 1
  `(0,9),(0,7),(0,8),(1,6),(-1,0)` and mode 2
  `(0,9),(1,7),(1,4),(1,1),(1,5),(0,8),(1,6),(-1,0)`. This transition path sets child
  `+0x18/+0x1b/+0x15`, not child `+5`; child creation starts with `+5=0`.
- Tooling:
  `tools/logh7_hud_admission_watch.py` now records `thisState` for `FUN_005015f0` events. Its
  non-default force path writes `thisEcx+5` and emits `force-this-gate05`; the older
  `--force-interaction-target-gate` remains only as a deprecated alias.
- Live caveat:
  `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-c002-this-gate-20260621e/` did not reach strategic UI. Screenshot stayed
  on the starfield, trace had only `scenario-seed` and `economy-seed`, and watcher output had no
  `inputHitTest-leave-005015f0`. Treat it as startup/cleanup evidence only, not C002 gate evidence.
- Evidence:
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-this-gate-static-correction-20260621e.md`.
  Verification: `python -m unittest tools.tests.test_logh7_hud_admission_watch` passed 6 tests and
  `python -m py_compile tools\logh7_hud_admission_watch.py tools\tests\test_logh7_hud_admission_watch.py`
  passed.

## 2026-06-21 - G006 C002 live HUD admission and bootstrap port correction

- Tooling correction:
  the canonical playable EXE contains `login-commandline-bootstrap`, which connects internally to
  `127.0.0.1:47900`. A live run started with `ui_explorer --port 47912` cannot receive conn1, but the
  harness previously marked `loggedIn=true` because it trusted the launch stack. `tools/logh7_ui_explorer.py`
  now rejects commandline bootstrap with any port other than `47900`; `tools.tests.test_logh7_ui_explorer`
  covers this.
- Live session:
  `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-c002-this-gate-live-20260621f-port47900/` reached the strategic HUD with
  terrain and star labels. Trace included `0x7000`, `0x200a`, `0x0201`, `0x0f02`, `0x0325/0x0323`,
  `0x0f03`, `0x0f07`, `0x0b09/0x0b0a`, `0x0356`, `0x1200/0x1202/0x1201`. Inputs produced only
  `0x0f08->0x0f09`; no `0x0b01` or `0x0b07`.
- Watcher result:
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-this-gate-live-20260621f.jsonl` captured 22,487
  `FUN_005015f0` leaves; every `retvalLow8` was `0`. The broad `thisState.gate05` distribution was
  `1:17737`, `0:4750`, so the prior "this gate is simply zero" model is incomplete.
- Selection owner correction:
  `FUN_004f6600` disassembly shows `004f663c mov ecx,[esi]` before `call 0x5015f0`, so selection row
  hit-test uses `selectionList[0]` as the `thisEcx` owner. Live role samples showed
  `selection-primary-0` and `selection-secondary-0` both had this owner `gate05=0`, while
  `listSelected189=-1`, `hudModeF4=1`, `hudAb0=-1`, `activeGate05=0`, `rowCountD4=24`,
  `selectedD5=-1`, and `categoryD6=-1` stayed fixed.
- Static mode path:
  `FUN_004f6680(selectionList, mode)` calls `FUN_005024b0(1)` on `selectionList[0]` only when `mode`
  is `1..3`; otherwise it returns. `FUN_004fd7a0` is the normal transition path that sets `HUD+0xf4`
  and calls `FUN_004f6680(1)`, but the live watcher saw `hudModeSet=0` and `hudModeF4=1` throughout.
- Next RE target:
  instrument `FUN_004fd100` around the `HUD+0x24/+0x28` mode activation hit-tests and record
  coordinates/outInfo/target state. Do not repeat server payload changes or broad `thisEcx+5` forcing
  until natural `FUN_004fd7a0(2,1)` or an equivalent transition is observed.
- Evidence:
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-this-gate-live-20260621f.md`,
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-c002-mode-target-live-20260621f.jsonl`,
  `.omo/ui-explorer/session-g006-c002-this-gate-live-20260621f-port47900/trace.jsonl`.
  Verification: `python -m unittest tools.tests.test_logh7_ui_explorer` passed 12 tests and
  `python -m py_compile tools\logh7_ui_explorer.py tools\tests\test_logh7_ui_explorer.py` passed.

- RE confirmation: `FUN_004f5cb0` reads category record `FUN_004c8700()+10+category*0x46` and copies `record+0x14` into row count; `FUN_005312b0` reads `FUN_004c8700()+category*0x46+0x20+selectedIndex*2` and only type `0x19/0x3f/0x40` enters move state. `FUN_004c4a10` is a one-shot promote: if `client+0x3416d8` guard is already nonzero it returns before copying transformed staging to runtime.

## 2026-06-21 - G006 planet data absence investigation

- Goal: explain why the star-system data surface appears to have no planets, using current content JSON, content SQLite, runtime world-state SQLite, and live server trace evidence.
- Hypotheses:
  H1: source content has no planet rows; distinguishing evidence is `content/galaxy.json`, runtime `galaxy.json`, and `logh7-content.db` planet counts.
  H2: planets exist in content, but the world-state star-system table intentionally strips nested planet arrays and stores planets in a separate economy/runtime table; distinguishing evidence is code path from `contentPack.systems` through `seedSystems` and `seedEconomyFromSystems`, plus runtime SQLite counts.
  H3: packaged runtime content is stale or mismatched versus source content; distinguishing evidence is source/runtime file hashes and count diffs.
- Artifacts to revert:
  - `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-planet-data-root-20260621j.mjs` - remove if not promoted.
  - `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-planet-data-root-20260621j.json` - remove if not promoted.
  - `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-planet-data-root-20260621j.md` - remove if not promoted.
- Result:
  H1 refuted: `content/galaxy.json`, packaged runtime `galaxy.json`, source content DB, and runtime
  content DB all have 80 systems / 281 planets / 77 systems with planets.
  H3 refuted for counts: packaged runtime content has the same system/planet counts as source.
  H2 supported: the latest real-client trace records `economy-seed planets=281 restored=true`, and
  both runtime SQLite snapshots preserve `world.systems[*].planets` plus `entities.economy.planets`.
  The visible "no planets in star-system data" symptom is a consumer/wire projection gap, not missing
  data. Strategic `0x0313/0x0315` consumes systems as map markers only; `0x031f` currently rolls
  planets into aggregate base/economy fields and does not serialize planet names/orbits.
  Evidence: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-planet-data-root-20260621j.md` and `.json`.

## 2026-06-21 - G006 NO DATA / glyph panel follow-up

- Live GDI probe was extended to capture both ANSI and UTF-16 GDI sinks (`ExtTextOutW`,
  `TextOutW`, `DrawTextW`, `GetTextExtentPoint32W`) while still preserving ANSI glyph-atlas
  backtraces. The post-fix capture is
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-nodata-gdi-text-no1202-20260621.json`, trace
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-nodata-gdi-trace-no1202-20260621.jsonl`, screenshot
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-nodata-gdi-shot-no1202-20260621.png`.
- Important negative evidence: visible `NO DATA` did not appear in either ANSI or W GDI text
  events. Do not treat the visible panels as confirmed consumers of `0x0356` or `0x1200/1201/1202`
  until the `FUN_00522010`/widget-string source path is hooked directly.
- The pre-fix live run showed malformed post-load simple-info, not missing simple-info:
  `Input_SimpleInformationCharacter::input_from_stream` rejected the current `0x1202` payload
  (`charged_base_size[9] is over than 4`, then `display_name_size[64/65] is over than 13`).
  Server default now keeps post-load `0x1200/0x1202/0x1201` disabled behind
  `LOGH_POSTLOAD_SIMPLE_INFO=1`; the verified post-fix trace contains `0x0356` but no `0x120x`,
  and the `0x1202` parser errors are gone. This is a removal of bad bytes, not a data-fill fix.
- RE/GDI path split:
  `FUN_004b0960` is the GDI atlas glyph builder (`GetTextExtentPoint32A`/`ExtTextOutA`);
  `FUN_004eb100` is the central text renderer; `FUN_004d8280 -> FUN_004ce350 -> FUN_004eb100`
  renders strategic map labels from constmsg group `0x18`; `FUN_0050b550`/`FUN_004e8b40`
  render widget/list text.
- The installed `data/MsgDat/constmsg.dat` group `0x18` decoded cleanly as CP949:
  subId 17=`발할라`, 64=`페잔`, 70=`볼솔른`, etc. Therefore the map labels themselves are
  not currently explained by a damaged local MsgDat record. The screenshot's broken suffix after
  `발할라` is on the widget/list path, not the strategic map label path.
- Residual errors after the simple-info fix: `_ERR:[Input_ResponseTacticsInformationUnitShip::input_from_stream]
  information_size[24832] is over than 600.` and unsupported `0x033b` remain. These are separate
  consumers to trace before sending richer ship/tactics records.

## 2026-06-21 - G006 NO DATA MsgDat source path and HUD label fix

- Added a source-level Frida probe, `tools/logh7_frida_msgdat_lookup.py`, because the visible
  `NO DATA` panels did not reach the GDI ANSI/W text sinks as literal text. The probe hooks
  `FUN_00522010` and `FUN_005229d0`, records group/sub-id, returned C string/hex, and a
  G7MTClient VA backtrace. Unit coverage: `tools/tests/test_logh7_frida_msgdat_lookup.py`.
- Live pre-fix capture:
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-msgdat-lookup-no1202-20260621.json`, trace
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-msgdat-lookup-trace-no1202-20260621.jsonl`, screenshot
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-msgdat-lookup-shot-no1202-20260621.png`.
  It recorded 501 events and 99 `NO DATA` returns:
  `group 0x68`=75, `group 0x6a`=15, `group 0x16`=8, `group 0x76`=1.
- Consumer split:
  - `group 0x68` came from `FUN_0058d140` / `FUN_0058ee70` right-detail/HUD label paths.
    Both original CAB JP and KO overlay `constmsg.dat` have group `0x68` size 3
    (`일제 사격`, `연속 사격`, `사격 정지`), while the callers request subIds up to `0x1a`.
    The consumed labels match constmsg group `0x63` (`작전`, `통솔`, `정치`, `운영`, `정보`,
    `지휘`, `기동`, `공격`, `방어`, `영향력`, `우주력`, `년`, `월`, `일`, `시`, `분`, etc.).
    This is a client MsgDat group-immediate bug, not a missing server `0x0356/0x120x` record.
  - `group 0x6a` came from `FUN_0054f680` menu/panel initialization. Original group `0x6a`
    has only six mission names (`방위 임무`..`철퇴 임무`), while the init code requests
    subIds `9..0x15`. This remains unresolved; do not patch it until the intended target group
    or data source is identified.
  - `group 0x16` came from `FUN_00544b20` command/mail/list formatting; `group 0x76` came
    from `FUN_004c2a80` strategic object/source enumeration. Both disappeared in the
    post-patch run, so they were not stable server-record blockers in this scenario.
- Applied same-length EXE patch `tools/client_patches/hud-msgdat-groupfix.json` and added it
  to the default playable stack in `tools/logh7_build_playable_client.py`. It flips 16
  drift-guarded `push 0x68` sites in `FUN_0058d140/FUN_0058ee70` to `push 0x63`.
  Drift test artifact: `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-hud-msgdat-groupfix-test-manifest.json`.
  Rebuilt and deployed playable EXE SHA `f83f7f74482f74d87b27fd476add74463803fe6ce23b3ab36dee3a2bdef3169c`.
- Live post-fix capture:
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-msgdat-lookup-hudfix-20260621.json`, trace
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-msgdat-lookup-hudfix-trace-20260621.jsonl`, screenshot
  `.omo/ulw-loop/evidence/g006-msgdat-lookup-hudfix-shot-20260621.png`.
  It recorded 159 events and 15 `NO DATA` returns, all `group 0x6a`; `group 0x68`,
  `group 0x16`, and `group 0x76` `NO DATA` returns were gone.
- Fixed CP949-visible broken glyph source bytes in the KO constmsg overlay and installed copy:
  `content/localization/constmsg-glyphfix-ko.json` maps flat record `1373` (`0x16/0x61`)
  from CP932-only `0x815e` to `/`, record `1374` (`0x16/0x62`) from CP932-only `0x81a6`
  to `※`, and records `1395/1396` from repeated CP932 full-width spaces (`0x8140`) to
  ordinary spaces. Re-encoded `.omo/work/logh7-ko-overlay/data/MsgDat/constmsg.dat` and
  `.omo/work/logh7-installed/data/MsgDat/constmsg.dat` with record count preserved at 3199.
  Decode verification now shows `/`, `※`, `%s                    %6d%s`, and
  `%s                 %3d%s` with no U+FFFD.
- Tests after changes:
  `python -m unittest tools.tests.test_logh7_msgdat_encode tools.tests.test_logh7_frida_gdi_text tools.tests.test_logh7_frida_msgdat_lookup`
  passed (12 tests). `node --test tests/server/logh7-login-session.test.mjs` passed (99 tests).

  - `DAT_00c9e638` holds a pointer to the allocated command-menu object (currently `0x11145210`);

    without writing state, indicating the required widgets (`0x67`, `0x6a`) are not active.
  - `FUN_004fd100` HUD update runs each frame, but `FUN_004f6b00` cannot resolve a category because
    `selectState` selection count is 0 and the source category table at `source+0x26c` is not being
    consumed.
  - With the strategic source cell patch (`0x4c4170` detour) already active, `targetValidator`
    `FUN_004d6310` is reached on synthetic clicks but returns `-256`; the projected X coordinate
    is garbage (`8074780`) because the click-to-grid projection branch is not satisfied, likely
    due to the same missing command-panel/selection-list activation.
- Conclusion: the remaining blocker for natural `0x0b01` is not the source cell, but activation of
  the command-panel widget group (`0x65`/`0x67`/`0x6a`) so that `FUN_004f68f0` runs naturally and
  `FUN_004f5cb0` populates `categoryD6`. Next step is either (a) identify the server message or
  client state that enables that widget group, or (b) a surgical runtime patch/cave that calls
  `FUN_004f68f0` only after verifying widget activation, rather than forcing it blindly.

## 2026-06-25 G196+ M1/M2 PoC: scene-setup patch enables HUD, selection-list activation remains the blocker

- Rebuilt canonical `G7MTClient.playable.exe` back to the default stack (no `login-commandline-bootstrap`, no `c002-force-*` patches) so `npm test` passes again. The temporary c002+autologin test build remains at `.omo/work/logh7-ko-overlay/exe/G7MTClient.playable-c002s-test.exe` for live probing.
- Confirmed `npm test` full suite passes: 347 Python + 1149 Node server tests + 3 Playwright.
- Two-client autologin world entry works when the server is started with `LOGH_POSTLOAD_ACTION_LIST_SEATS=1` and the c002-force-scene-setup patch is present; without the patch, autologin clients fall back to the login form with garbled account text.
- Live memory state with c002-force-scene-setup:
  - `DAT_00c9e768` command-menu object is allocated, `categoryD6=0`, `rowCountD4=0`, `selectedD5=0`.
  - `DAT_00c9eac4` selection-list object is allocated but `listCount=0`, `listSelected=0`, `payload=null`.
  - Writing `HUD+0xab0` (absolute `0x00c9e6e8`) from `-1` to `0` triggers `FUN_004f68f0` and populates `selectionList+0x620` to `1`, proving the payload at `*(DAT_007ccffc+8)+0x270` is already valid.
  - However, the per-frame category-application path does not populate command-menu rows (`rowCountD4` stays `0`). Direct calls to `FUN_004f5cb0` and `FUN_004f68f0` from Frida crash with access violations, confirming the objects need natural widget-route activation rather than raw function calls.
- Hypothesis update: the remaining blocker for natural `0x0b01` is not payload count, but the client-side activation of the selection-list/command-row widget route. Two candidate fixes:
  1. Server-side: send the `0x0356` character delta with a nonzero actionable `seatRole` or set `LOGH_ACTION_LIST_CATEGORY=0` so `FUN_004f6b00` resolves category `0` and `FUN_004f5cb0` builds command rows.
  2. Client-side: extend the c002-force-scene-setup patch (or add a new `c002-force-selection-list` patch) so `FUN_004fc4e0`/`FUN_004f6040` create/refresh the selection-list widget `0x6a` on the active HUD root, not just the command-menu widget `0x67`.
- Next step: test the combination `c002-force-scene-setup` + `LOGH_ACTION_LIST_CATEGORY=0` with a patched autologin EXE. The multiclient harness currently forces the canonical playable source; either add a `--patched-exe` option or manually spawn the two patched autologin clients.
